            }).createNewSupplier(name);
        }

        // --- BOM TAB ---
        function loadBomTab() { 
            // Chỉ khởi tạo Select2 một lần
            if (!$('#costProductName').data('select2')) {
                $('#bomProduct').select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', width: '100%' }); 
                $('#bomMaterial').select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', width: '100%' }); 
                $('#costProductName').select2({ 
                    theme: 'bootstrap-5', 
                    width: '100%',
                    tags: true,
                    placeholder: "-- Chọn hoặc nhập tên SP --",
                    allowClear: true,
                    insertTag: function (data, tag) {
                        // Insert the tag at the end of the results
                        data.push(tag);
                    }
                });
            }
            loadBOMData(); 
            loadLaborBOMData(); 
            loadActiveOrdersForCosting();
        }
        
        function loadActiveOrdersForCosting() {
            console.log("Costing: Requesting active orders...");
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_prod');
            if (cached) {
                try {
                    const orders = JSON.parse(cached);
                    if (orders && orders.length > 0) {
                        console.log("Costing: Loading from cache (" + orders.length + ")");
                        populateCostingDropdown(orders);
                    }
                } catch(e) { console.error("Cache Error:", e); }
            }

            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(orders => {
                    console.log("Costing: Server returned", orders ? orders.length : 0, "orders");
                    if (orders && Array.isArray(orders)) {
                        localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_prod', JSON.stringify(orders));
                        populateCostingDropdown(orders);
                    }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(err => {
                    console.error("Costing: Server error", err);
                    showMsg("Lỗi tải danh sách đơn hàng cho Định mức: " + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getActiveOrders();
        }

        function populateCostingDropdown(orders) {
            console.log("Populating costing dropdown with", orders ? orders.length : 0, "entries");
            if (orders && orders.length > 0) console.table(orders.slice(0, 5)); // Log top 5 for debug

            window.activeOrdersForCosting = orders;
            const $select = $('#costProductName');
            
            // Khởi tạo Select2 nếu chưa có
            if (!$select.data('select2')) {
                $select.select2({ 
                    theme: 'bootstrap-5', 
                    width: '100%',
                    tags: true,
                    placeholder: "-- Chọn hoặc nhập tên SP --",
                    allowClear: true,
                    insertTag: function (data, tag) {
                        data.push(tag);
                    }
                });
            }

            const currentVal = $select.val();
            $select.empty();
            $select.append(new Option("-- Chọn sản phẩm --", "", true, true));
            
            if (orders && Array.isArray(orders) && orders.length > 0) {
                orders.forEach(o => {
                    const text = `#${o.id} - ${o.product} (${o.customer})`;
                    $select.append(new Option(text, o.id, false, false));
                });
            } else {
                // Nếu rỗng, hiển thị một option thông báo
                $select.append(new Option("(Không có đơn hàng đang chạy)", "", false, false));
            }
            
            if (currentVal) $select.val(currentVal);
            $select.trigger('change');
        }

        function updateCostProductDetails() {
            const orderId = document.getElementById('costProductName').value;
            if (!orderId || !window.activeOrdersForCosting) return;
            
            const order = window.activeOrdersForCosting.find(o => o.id == orderId);
            if (order) {
                document.getElementById('costOrderQty').value = order.qty;
                if (order.image) {
                    const imgUrl = getSafeImgUrl(order.image);
                    const box = document.getElementById('imgPreviewBox');
                    box.style.backgroundImage = `url(${imgUrl}=s400)`;
                    box.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
                    box.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
                    box.innerHTML = '<input type="file" id="costProductImg" class="d-none" onchange="previewCostingImg(this)">';
                }
                calculateFullCosting();
                
                // Tự động kiểm tra định mức cũ (Chỉ lấy tên SP chuẩn)
                const productName = order.product;
                console.log("Checking historical BOM for:", productName);
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(async oldBOM => {
                    console.log("Result from server:", oldBOM);
                    if (oldBOM) {
                        if (await showConfirm(`Hệ thống tìm thấy định mức cũ của [${productName}]. Bạn có muốn tải lại không?`)) {
                            applyBOMData(oldBOM);
                        }
                    }
                }).getBOMDetail(productName);
            }
        }

        function loadHistoricalBOM() {
            const $select = $('#costProductName');
            // Lấy tên sản phẩm chuẩn từ dữ liệu đơn hàng đã tải
            const orderId = $select.val();
            let productName = "";
            
            if (orderId && window.activeOrdersForCosting) {
                const order = window.activeOrdersForCosting.find(o => o.id == orderId);
                if (order) productName = order.product;
            } else {
                productName = $select.val(); // Nếu tự nhập
            }
            
            if (!productName || productName.includes("-- Chọn")) return alert("Vui lòng chọn hoặc nhập tên sản phẩm trước!");

            console.log("Manual search for:", productName);
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(oldBOM => {
                if (oldBOM) {
                    applyBOMData(oldBOM);
                    showMsg("✅ Đã tải lại định mức cũ của: " + productName);
                } else {
                    showMsg("❌ Không tìm thấy định mức cũ của: " + productName, 'warning');
                }
            }).getBOMDetail(productName);
        }

        function copyBOMFromOther() {
            const modal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('copyBOMModal'));
            modal.show();
            document.getElementById('copyBOMListBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center py-4"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-primary"></div> Đang tải dữ liệu...</td></tr>';
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                window.allSavedBOMs = list;
                renderCopyBOMList(list);
            }).getSavedBOMList();
        }

        function renderCopyBOMList(list) {
            const body = document.getElementById('copyBOMListBody');
            if (!list || list.length === 0) {
                body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center py-4 text-muted">Chưa có sản phẩm nào có định mức lưu trong hệ thống.</td></tr>';
                return;
            }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(item => {
                h += `<tr>
                    <td class="small fw-bold">${item.productName}</td>
                    <td class="small text-center text-muted">${item.updatedAt}</td>
                    <td class="text-center">
                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary py-0" onclick="selectBOMToCopy('${item.productName}')">Chọn</button>
                    </td>
                </tr>`;
            });
            body.innerHTML = h;
        }

        function filterCopyBOMList() {
            const query = document.getElementById('searchCopyBOM').value.toLowerCase().trim();
            if (!window.allSavedBOMs) return;
            const filtered = window.allSavedBOMs.filter(i => i.productName.toLowerCase().includes(query));
            renderCopyBOMList(filtered);
        }

        function selectBOMToCopy(productName) {
            bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('copyBOMModal')).hide();
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(oldBOM => {
                if (oldBOM) {
                    applyBOMData(oldBOM);
                    showMsg(`✅ Đã copy định mức từ [${productName}] thành công!`);
                } else {
                    showMsg("❌ Không tìm thấy mẫu định mức của sản phẩm này.", 'error');
                }
            }).getBOMDetail(productName);
        }

        function applyBOMData(data) {
            // 1. Vải
            const fabricBody = document.getElementById('fabricRows');
            fabricBody.innerHTML = "";
            if (data.fabrics && data.fabrics.length > 0) {
                data.fabrics.forEach(f => {
                    addFabricRow(f);
                });
            }

            // 2. Công đoạn
            const stageBody = document.getElementById('stageRows');
            stageBody.innerHTML = "";
            if (data.stages && data.stages.length > 0) {
                data.stages.forEach(st => {
                    addStageRow(st);
                });
            }
            
            // 3. Margin
            if (data.margin) document.getElementById('costMargin').value = data.margin;

            calculateFullCosting();
        }
        
        // Vật tư
        function loadBOMData() { document.getElementById('bomList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center">Đang tải...</td></tr>'; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(renderBOM).getBOMList(); }
        function renderBOM(list) {
            const tb = document.getElementById('bomList');
            if (list.length === 0) { tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center text-muted">Chưa có định mức nào.</td></tr>'; return; }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(i => { h += `<tr><td data-label="Sản phẩm">${i.product}</td><td data-label="Vật tư">${i.material}</td><td data-label="ĐVT">${i.unit}</td><td data-label="Định mức">${i.qty}</td><td data-label="Thao tác" class="text-center"><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger border-0" onclick="deleteBOM(${i.id})"><i class="bi bi-trash"></i></button></td></tr>`; });
            tb.innerHTML = h;
        }
        function submitBOM() {
            const p = document.getElementById('bomProduct').value; const m = document.getElementById('bomMaterial').value;
            const u = document.getElementById('bomUnit').value; const q = document.getElementById('bomQty').value;
            if (!p || !m || !q) { alert("Thiếu thông tin!"); return; }
            const btn = event.target; btn.innerText = "..."; btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { showMsg(res); btn.innerText = "THÊM ĐỊNH MỨC VẬT TƯ"; btn.disabled = false; $('#bomMaterial').val(null).trigger('change'); document.getElementById('bomUnit').value = ""; document.getElementById('bomQty').value = ""; loadBOMData(); }).saveBOM({ product: p, material: m, unit: u, qty: q });
        }
        async function deleteBOM(id) { if (!(await showConfirm("Xóa dòng định mức này?"))) return; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { loadBOMData(); }).deleteBOM(id); }

        // Nhân công
        function loadLaborBOMData() { document.getElementById('laborBomList').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center">Đang tải...</td></tr>'; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(renderLaborBOM).getLaborBOMList(); }
        function renderLaborBOM(list) {
            const tb = document.getElementById('laborBomList');
            if (list.length === 0) { tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center text-muted">Chưa có định mức nhân công nào.</td></tr>'; return; }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(i => { h += `<tr><td data-label="Sản phẩm">${i.product}</td><td data-label="Công đoạn">${i.stage}</td><td data-label="Đơn giá" class="fw-bold text-primary">${Number(i.price).toLocaleString()} đ</td><td data-label="Xóa" class="text-center"><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger border-0" onclick="deleteLaborBOM(${i.id})"><i class="bi bi-trash"></i></button></td></tr>`; });
            tb.innerHTML = h;
        }
        function submitLaborBOM() {
            const p = document.getElementById('bomProduct').value;
            const s = document.getElementById('laborStage').value;
            const pr = document.getElementById('laborPrice').value;
            if (!p || !s || !pr) return alert("Thiếu thông tin!");
            const btn = event.target; btn.innerText = "..."; btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { 
                showMsg(res); btn.innerText = "THÊM ĐỊNH MỨC NHÂN CÔNG"; btn.disabled = false; 
                document.getElementById('laborPrice').value = ""; 
                loadLaborBOMData(); 
            }).saveLaborBOM({ product: p, stage: s, price: pr });
        }
        async function deleteLaborBOM(id) { if (!(await showConfirm("Xóa định mức nhân công này?"))) return; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { loadLaborBOMData(); }).deleteLaborBOM(id); }

        // Tính toán
        function viewProductCost() {
            const p = document.getElementById('bomProduct').value; if (!p) return alert("Chọn sản phẩm trước!");
            document.getElementById('costDisplay').innerText = "Đang tính...";
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                if (res.error) { 
                    alert(res.error); 
                    document.getElementById('costDisplay').innerText = "Lỗi!";
                } else { 
                    document.getElementById('costDisplay').innerText = res.totalCost + " VNĐ"; 
                    showCostBreakdown(res);
                }
            }).withFailureHandler(err => {
                alert("Lỗi server: " + err);
                document.getElementById('costDisplay').innerText = "Lỗi!";
            }).calculateProductCost(p);
        }

        function showCostBreakdown(data) {
            document.getElementById('cbProductName').innerText = data.productName;
            
            // Render Materials
            let matH = "";
            if (data.materialDetails && data.materialDetails.length > 0) {
                data.materialDetails.forEach(m => {
                    matH += `<tr><td>${m.name}</td><td>${m.qty}</td><td>${Number(m.price).toLocaleString()}</td><td class="fw-bold">${Number(m.total).toLocaleString()}</td></tr>`;
                });
            }
            document.getElementById('cbMaterialTable').innerHTML = matH || '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center text-muted">Không có dữ liệu vật tư</td></tr>';
            document.getElementById('cbMaterialTotal').innerText = Number(data.materialCost).toLocaleString();

            // Render Labor
            let labH = "";
            if (data.laborDetails && data.laborDetails.length > 0) {
                data.laborDetails.forEach(l => {
                    labH += `<tr><td>${l.stage}</td><td class="fw-bold text-primary">${Number(l.price).toLocaleString()}</td></tr>`;
                });
            }
            document.getElementById('cbLaborTable').innerHTML = labH || '<tr><td colspan="2" class="text-center text-muted">Không có dữ liệu nhân công</td></tr>';
            document.getElementById('cbLaborTotal').innerText = Number(data.laborCost).toLocaleString();

            document.getElementById('cbOverheadTotal').innerText = Number(data.overheadCost).toLocaleString();
            document.getElementById('cbGrandTotal').innerText = data.totalCost + " VNĐ";

            // Hiển thị modal (sử dụng cả BS5 vanilla và jQuery fallback)
            const modalEl = document.getElementById('costBreakdownModal');
            try {
                const m = new bootstrap.Modal(modalEl);
                m.show();
            } catch (e) {
                console.log("Bootstrap Modal error, trying jQuery:", e);
                if (window.jQuery && $(modalEl).modal) {
                    $(modalEl).modal('show');
                } else {
                    alert("Không thể mở bảng chi tiết. Vui lòng kiểm tra lại hệ thống.");
                }
            }
        }

        function resetCostView() { document.getElementById('costDisplay').innerText = "--- VNĐ"; }

        // --- QR SCAN & PROD ---
        let whQrScanner = null;
        function openWhScanModal() { new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('whScanModal')).show(); setTimeout(() => { document.getElementById('wh-reader').innerHTML = ""; whQrScanner = new Html5Qrcode("wh-reader"); whQrScanner.start({ facingMode: "environment" }, { fps: 10, qrbox: { width: 250, height: 250 } }, (decodedText) => { whQrScanner.stop().then(() => { bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('whScanModal')).hide(); $('#whMat').val(decodedText).trigger('change'); document.getElementById('whQty').focus(); }).catch(err => console.log(err)); }); }, 500); }
        $('#whScanModal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () { if (whQrScanner) try { whQrScanner.stop(); } catch (e) { } });
        function openCalcModal() { new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('calcModal')).show(); }
        function runCalc() {
            const p = document.getElementById('calcProduct').value; const q = document.getElementById('calcQty').value;
            if (!p || !q) return; document.getElementById('calcResult').innerHTML = "Đang tính...";
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                if (res.error) { document.getElementById('calcResult').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-warning">${res.error}</div>`; return; }
                let h = '<table class="table table-bordered table-sm small"><thead><tr><th>Vật tư</th><th>Cần</th><th>Tồn</th><th>Trạng thái</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                res.list.forEach(i => { let cls = i.isOk ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger fw-bold'; h += `<tr><td>${i.material}</td><td>${i.need}</td><td>${i.stock}</td><td class="${cls}">${i.status}</td></tr>`; });
                h += '</tbody></table>'; document.getElementById('calcResult').innerHTML = h;
            }).calculateMaterials(p, q);
        }

        // --- OTHER FUNCS ---
        function initReportDates() { const d = new Date(); const m = d.getMonth() + 1; const y = d.getFullYear(); const mSelect = document.getElementById('rptMonth'); if (mSelect) mSelect.value = m; const ySelect = document.getElementById('rptYear'); if (ySelect) { ySelect.innerHTML = "";[y - 1, y, y + 1].forEach(year => { let opt = new Option(year, year); if (year === y) opt.selected = true; ySelect.add(opt); }); } }
        function genReport() { const m = document.getElementById('rptMonth').value; const y = document.getElementById('rptYear').value; const btn = event.target.closest('button'); const originalText = btn.innerHTML; btn.innerHTML = "..."; btn.disabled = true; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(url => { btn.innerHTML = originalText; btn.disabled = false; window.open(url, '_blank'); }).withFailureHandler(err => { alert("Lỗi: " + err); btn.innerHTML = originalText; btn.disabled = false; }).createSalesReport(m, y); }
        function subOrd() {
            const b = document.getElementById('bs'), f = document.getElementById('orderForm');
            if (!f.checkValidity()) { f.reportValidity(); return; }
            b.disabled = true; b.innerText = "...";
            const pName = document.querySelector('input[name="productName"]').value;
            const cName = document.querySelector('select[name="customer"]').value;
            const qty = document.querySelector('input[name="quantity"]').value;
            const imgName = removeVietnameseTones(pName) + "_" + removeVietnameseTones(cName) + "_" + qty + ".jpg";
            const d = { 
                orderDate: f.orderDate.value, 
                customer: f.customer.value, 
                salesRep: f.salesRep.value, 
                productName: f.productName.value, 
                quantity: f.quantity.value, 
                salesPrice: document.querySelector('input[name="salesPrice"]').value, 
                deadline: f.deadline.value, 
                address: f.address.value, 
                phone: document.querySelector('input[name="phone"]').value, 
                notes: f.notes.value, 
                imageData: document.getElementById('id').value, 
                imageName: imgName 
            };
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(m => {
                    showMsg("✅ " + m);
                    f.reset();
                    document.getElementById('id').value = "";
                    document.getElementById('pi').style.display = "none";
                    f.orderDate.value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
                    document.getElementById('sm').innerText = m;
                    b.disabled = false; b.innerText = "LÊN ĐƠN";
                    document.getElementById('addrSuggestions').innerHTML = "";
                    setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('sm').innerText = "", 4000);
                    loadSalesHistory();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(err => {
                    showMsg("❌ Lỗi: " + (err.message || String(err)), 'error');
                    b.disabled = false; b.innerText = "LÊN ĐƠN";
                })
                .submitOrder(d);
        }
        function loadSalesHistory() {
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_sales');
            if (cached) renderSalesList(JSON.parse(cached));

            document.getElementById('salesHistoryList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></div>';
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_sales', JSON.stringify(data));
                renderSalesList(data);
            }).getSalesHistory();
        }
        function renderSalesList(orders) {
            const container = document.getElementById('salesHistoryList'); if (!orders || orders.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-secondary m-3 text-center">Chưa có đơn hàng nào.</div>'; return; }
            let html = '<table class="table table-custom table-mobile-cards"><thead><tr><th>Mã</th><th>Ngày</th><th>Khách</th><th>Sản phẩm</th><th>SL</th><th>Trạng thái</th><th>#</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
            orders.forEach(o => {
                const canEdit = (o.status === "Chờ cọc" || o.status === "Chờ xử lý"); const btnClass = canEdit ? "btn-warning" : "btn-secondary disabled";
                let stClass = "text-muted"; if (o.status.includes('Chờ')) stClass = "text-warning fw-bold"; if (o.status.includes('Đang') || o.status.includes('Sẵn sàng')) stClass = "text-primary fw-bold"; if (o.status.includes('Giao') || o.status.includes('Đã')) stClass = "text-success fw-bold"; if (o.status.includes('Hủy')) stClass = "text-danger text-decoration-line-through";
                const isCallOff = (o.salesRep === "Hệ thống (Call-off)");
                const callOffBadge = isCallOff ? '<span class="badge bg-info ms-1" style="font-size:9px">HĐ Khung</span>' : '';
                const rowClass = isCallOff ? "table-info" : "";
                
                // Format date for display
                const dParts = o.date.split('-');
                const displayDate = dParts.length === 3 ? `${dParts[2]}/${dParts[1]}/${dParts[0]}` : o.date;
                
                const dataStr = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(o));
                html += `<tr class="${rowClass}"><td data-label="Mã đơn" class="fw-bold text-primary">#${o.id}${callOffBadge}</td><td data-label="Ngày">${displayDate}</td><td data-label="Khách hàng">${o.customer}</td><td data-label="Sản phẩm">${o.product}</td><td data-label="Số lượng" class="text-center fw-bold">${o.qty}</td><td data-label="Trạng thái" class="${stClass}">${o.status}</td><td data-label="Sửa"><button class="btn btn-sm ${btnClass}" onclick="openEditModal('${dataStr}')"><i class="bi bi-pencil-square"></i></button></td></tr>`;
            });
            html += '</tbody></table>'; container.innerHTML = html;
        }

        // --- COPY ORDER FEATURE ---
        function openCopyOrderModal() {
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('copyOrderModal')).show();
            document.getElementById('copyOrderListBody').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-4"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-primary"></div> Đang tải dữ liệu...</td></tr>';
            
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_sales');
            if (cached) {
                window.allSalesHistory = JSON.parse(cached);
                renderCopyOrderList(window.allSalesHistory);
            }
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_sales', JSON.stringify(data));
                window.allSalesHistory = data;
                renderCopyOrderList(data);
            }).getSalesHistory();
        }

        function renderCopyOrderList(list) {
            const body = document.getElementById('copyOrderListBody');
            if (!list || list.length === 0) {
                body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center py-4 text-muted">Chưa có đơn hàng nào trong lịch sử.</td></tr>';
                return;
            }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(o => {
                h += `<tr>
                    <td class="fw-bold text-primary">#${o.id}</td>
                    <td class="small">${o.customer}</td>
                    <td class="small fw-bold">${o.product}</td>
                    <td class="small text-success fw-bold">${Number(o.price || 0).toLocaleString()}</td>
                    <td class="text-center">
                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary py-0 px-3 btn-round" onclick="selectOrderToCopy('${o.id}')">Copy</button>
                    </td>
                </tr>`;
            });
            body.innerHTML = h;
        }

        function filterCopyOrderList() {
            const query = document.getElementById('searchCopyOrder').value.toLowerCase().trim();
            if (!window.allSalesHistory) return;
            const filtered = window.allSalesHistory.filter(o => 
                o.id.toString().includes(query) || 
                o.customer.toLowerCase().includes(query) || 
                o.product.toLowerCase().includes(query)
            );
            renderCopyOrderList(filtered);
        }

        function selectOrderToCopy(orderId) {
            const order = window.allSalesHistory.find(o => o.id == orderId);
            if (!order) return;
            
            bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('copyOrderModal')).hide();
            
            const form = document.getElementById('orderForm');
            // Populate form
            $('#customerSelect').val(order.customer).trigger('change');
            $('#salesSelect').val(order.salesRep).trigger('change');
            form.productName.value = order.product;
            form.quantity.value = order.qty;
            form.salesPrice.value = order.price;
            form.address.value = order.address || "";
            form.phone.value = order.phone || "";
            form.notes.value = order.notes || "";
            
            // Highlight effect for the card
            const card = form.closest('.card-custom');
            card.classList.add('border-primary');
            setTimeout(() => card.classList.remove('border-primary'), 2000);
            
            showMsg(`Đã copy dữ liệu từ đơn #${orderId}. Hãy kiểm tra lại ngày tháng và nhấn LÊN ĐƠN.`);
        }

        function openEditModal(dataStr) { const o = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(dataStr)); document.getElementById('editId').value = o.id; document.getElementById('editIdDisplay').innerText = o.id; setFlatpickrDate('editDeadline', o.deadline); document.getElementById('editProductName').value = o.product; document.getElementById('editQuantity').value = o.qty; document.getElementById('editPrice').value = o.price; document.getElementById('editAddress').value = o.address; document.getElementById('editPhone').value = o.phone; document.getElementById('editNotes').value = o.notes; const custSelect = document.getElementById('editCustomerSelect'); const saleSelect = document.getElementById('editSalesSelect'); custSelect.innerHTML = document.getElementById('customerSelect').innerHTML; saleSelect.innerHTML = document.getElementById('salesSelect').innerHTML; custSelect.value = o.customer; saleSelect.value = o.salesRep; new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('editOrderModal')).show(); }
        async function submitEditOrder() { if (!(await showConfirm("Lưu thay đổi?"))) return; const form = document.getElementById('editOrderForm'); const btn = document.querySelector('#editOrderModal .btn-primary'); const data = { id: form.id.value, customer: form.customer.value, salesRep: form.salesRep.value, productName: form.productName.value, quantity: form.quantity.value, salesPrice: form.salesPrice.value, deadline: form.deadline.value, address: form.address.value, phone: form.phone.value, notes: form.notes.value }; btn.innerText = "..."; btn.disabled = true; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { showMsg(res); btn.innerText = "LƯU THAY ĐỔI"; btn.disabled = false; bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('editOrderModal')).hide(); loadSalesHistory(); }).editOrder(data); }
        function updateEditAddress() { const n = document.getElementById('editCustomerSelect').value; const as = window.customerMap[n] || []; if (as.length > 0 && as[0] !== "") document.getElementById('editAddress').value = as[0]; }
        function updateAddress() { const n = document.getElementById('customerSelect').value; const as = window.customerMap[n] || []; const inp = document.getElementById('addrInput'); const sug = document.getElementById('addrSuggestions'); inp.value = ""; sug.innerHTML = ""; if (as.length === 1 && as[0] !== "") { inp.value = as[0]; } else if (as.length > 1) { let h = "<small class='text-muted d-block mb-1 w-100'>Gợi ý kho:</small>"; as.forEach(a => { h += "<button type=\"button\" class=\"btn btn-outline-primary btn-sm rounded-pill\" onclick=\"document.getElementById('addrInput').value='" + a + "'\">" + a + "</button>"; }); sug.innerHTML = h; } }
        function loadProductionData() {
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_prod');
            if (cached) ro(JSON.parse(cached));

            document.getElementById('ol').innerHTML = "";
            document.getElementById('lp').style.display = "block";
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_prod', JSON.stringify(data));
                ro(data);
            }).getActiveOrders();
        }

        let ganttTimeline = null;
        function loadGantt() {
            const loader = document.getElementById('loading-gantt');
            if (loader) loader.style.display = 'block';
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                if (loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
                renderGantt(data);
            }).getGanttData();
        }
        function renderGantt(data) {
            const container = document.getElementById('gantt-visualization');
            if (!container) return;
            
            // Sắp xếp data theo độ ưu tiên trước khi hiển thị
            data.sort((a, b) => (b.priorityScore || 0) - (a.priorityScore || 0));

            const groups = new vis.DataSet();
            const items = new vis.DataSet();
            data.forEach(order => {
                const progress = order.progress || 0;
                const isUrgent = order.isUrgent || order.priority;
                const colorClass = isUrgent ? 'bg-danger' : 'bg-primary';
                const groupContent = `<div class="gantt-group-wrapper"><div class="gantt-group-title"><span>#${order.id} - ${order.customer}</span><span class="badge ${colorClass}">${progress}%</span></div><div class="gantt-group-subtitle">${order.product} (SL: ${order.qty})</div><div class="gantt-progress-container"><div class="gantt-progress-fill ${colorClass}" style="width: ${progress}%"></div></div></div>`;
                groups.add({ id: order.id, content: groupContent });
                
                let itemColor = '#3b82f6'; // Blue
                if (order.status.includes('Sẵn sàng')) itemColor = '#10b981'; // Green
                if (order.status.includes('Chờ')) itemColor = '#f59e0b'; // Amber
                if (isUrgent) itemColor = '#ef4444'; // Red
                
                items.add({ id: order.id, group: order.id, content: `Đơn ${order.id}`, start: order.start, end: order.end, style: `background-color: ${itemColor}; border-color: ${itemColor};` });
            });
            const options = { stack: false, verticalScroll: true, zoomKey: 'ctrlKey', orientation: 'top', start: new Date(new Date().getTime() - 3 * 86400000), end: new Date(new Date().getTime() + 14 * 86400000), editable: false, margin: { item: 10, axis: 5 } };
            if (ganttTimeline) { ganttTimeline.setGroups(groups); ganttTimeline.setItems(items); }
            else { ganttTimeline = new vis.Timeline(container, items, groups, options); }
        }
        function moveGantt(dir) {
            if (!ganttTimeline) return;
            const range = ganttTimeline.getWindow();
            const interval = range.end - range.start;
            if (dir === 'prev') { ganttTimeline.setWindow(range.start.getTime() - interval, range.end.getTime() - interval); }
            else if (dir === 'next') { ganttTimeline.setWindow(range.start.getTime() + interval, range.end.getTime() + interval); }
            else if (dir === 'today') { const now = new Date().getTime(); ganttTimeline.setWindow(now - 3 * 86400000, now + 14 * 86400000); }
        }
        function getSafeImgUrl(url) { url = (url || "").toString().trim(); if (!url) return ""; if (url.includes("drive.google.com") || url.includes("googleusercontent")) { const match = url.match(/[-\w]{25,}/); if (match) return "https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/d/" + match[0]; } return url; }
        function adjQ(id, delta, max) { 
            const input = document.getElementById('q-' + id); 
            let val = parseInt(input.value) || 0; 
            val += delta; 
            if (val < 0) val = 0; 
            if (val > max) val = max; 
            input.value = val; 
        }
        function setQ(id, val) { 
            document.getElementById('q-' + id).value = val; 
        }

        function ro(os) {
            document.getElementById('lp').style.display = "none";
            const c = document.getElementById('ol');

            // Nút quét QR nhập nhanh, Đồng bộ Lịch và Mở Lịch
            let h = '<div class="row g-2 mb-3">' +
                    '<div class="col-12"><button class="btn btn-dark w-100 fw-bold py-3 shadow" onclick="openScanModal()"><i class="bi bi-qr-code-scan"></i> QUÉT MÃ QR (NHẬP NHANH)</button></div>' +
                    '<div class="col-6"><button class="btn btn-outline-primary w-100 fw-bold py-2 shadow" onclick="syncCalendar()"><i class="bi bi-calendar-check"></i> ĐỒNG BỘ LỊCH</button></div>' +
                    '<div class="col-6"><a href="https://calendar.google.com/calendar/u/0?cid=ZHV5cGhhbUA0ZmludGVyY29tLmNvbQ" target="_blank" class="btn btn-outline-success w-100 fw-bold py-2 shadow d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center"><i class="bi bi-calendar-range me-2"></i> MỞ LỊCH</a></div>' +
                    '</div>';

            // Ẩn nút Lưu tiến độ với Thợ
            if (window.currentRole === 'worker') {
                const saveBtn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="saveAllProgress()"]');
                if (saveBtn) saveBtn.style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                const saveBtn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="saveAllProgress()"]');
                if (saveBtn) saveBtn.style.display = 'block';
            }

            if (!os || os.length === 0) {
                c.innerHTML = h + "<div class='text-center py-5 text-muted'>Không có đơn đang sản xuất.</div>";
                return;
            }

            // 1. SẮP XẾP: THEO ĐIỂM ƯU TIÊN TỰ ĐỘNG (MỚI)
            os.sort((a, b) => (b.priorityScore || 0) - (a.priorityScore || 0) || String(b.id).localeCompare(String(a.id)));

            h += '<div class="row g-3">';

            // Quyền chỉnh sửa ngày và Ưu tiên
            const canEdit = (window.currentRole === 'ceo' || window.currentRole === 'sale');
            const dateDisabled = canEdit ? "" : "disabled";
            const dateStyle = canEdit ? "border: 2px solid #3b82f6; color:#3b82f6; font-weight:bold" : "background-color:transparent; border:none; padding:0; font-weight:bold";

            os.forEach(o => {
                if (!o.progressDetail) o.progressDetail = { "Cắt": 0, "May": 0, "Thêu": 0, "Bơm": 0, "Đóng gói (đóng bao/dán mắt)": 0, "Khâu tay": 0 };
                var finalImgSrc = getSafeImgUrl(o.image);
                var qrData = JSON.stringify({ id: o.id, product: o.name, total: o.qty });
                var qrUrl = "https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=200x200&data=" + encodeURIComponent(qrData);
                var imgDisplay = (finalImgSrc) ? `<div class="img-thumb-container"><img src="${finalImgSrc}=s1000" class="img-thumb" onclick="sl('${finalImgSrc}=s3000')"></div>` : '';
                var pct = (o.qty > 0) ? Math.floor((o.done / o.qty) * 100) : 0; if (pct > 100) pct = 100;
                var remaining = o.qty - o.done;

                const isCallOff = (o.salesRep === "Hệ thống (Call-off)");
                const callOffTag = isCallOff ? '<span class="badge bg-info shadow-sm py-1 px-2 mb-1 d-inline-block" style="font-size: 10px; border-radius: 4px;"><i class="bi bi-link-45deg"></i> HĐ KHUNG</span><br>' : '';


                let urgentBadge = "";
                if (o.isUrgent) {
                    urgentBadge = `<span class="badge bg-warning text-dark shadow-sm py-1 px-2 mb-1 d-inline-block" style="font-size: 10px; border-radius: 4px;"><i class="bi bi-exclamation-triangle-fill"></i> GẤP</span> `;
                }


                let priorityBtn = "";
                if (o.priority) {
                    if (canEdit) priorityBtn = `<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm fw-bold shadow-sm" onclick="tS('${o.id}',this)">🔥 ƯU TIÊN</button>`;
                    else priorityBtn = `<span class="badge bg-danger p-2">🔥 ƯU TIÊN</span>`;
                } else {
                    if (canEdit) priorityBtn = `<button class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm fw-bold border-0" onclick="tS('${o.id}',this)"><i class="bi bi-star"></i> Chọn ưu tiên</button>`;
                }

                let borderClass = o.priority ? 'border-danger border-2' : '';
                if (isCallOff && !o.priority) borderClass = 'border-info border-2 shadow-sm';
                
                let bgStyle = o.priority ? 'background:#fff5f5;' : '';
                if (isCallOff && !o.priority) bgStyle = 'background:#f0faff;';

                let dateDisplay = canEdit 
                    ? `<input type="date" class="form-control form-control-sm" style="${dateStyle}" value="${o.deadlineRaw}" onchange="updateDead('${o.id}', this.value)">`
                    : `<span class="fw-bold text-primary" style="font-size: 1.1rem;">${o.deadline || '---'}</span>`;

                h += `<div class="col-md-6 col-xl-4">
                <div class="card-custom h-100 border ${borderClass}" style="${bgStyle}">
                    <div class="card-body-custom">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-2">
                            <div style="flex:1">
                                <div class="text-muted small">${urgentBadge}${callOffTag}#${o.id} | ${o.customer}</div>
                                <div class="prod-card-title text-primary">${o.name}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="ms-2">${priorityBtn}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="d-flex align-items-center mb-2 bg-light p-2 rounded">
                            <span class="small text-muted me-2">Giao hàng:</span>${dateDisplay}
                        </div>
                        ${imgDisplay}
                        
                        ${(function() {
                            const isManager = (window.currentRole === 'ceo' || window.currentRole === 'sale' || window.currentRole === 'prod');
                            let noteText = o.note || "";
                            if (isCallOff && o.note) {
                                const match = o.note.match(/💬 Ghi chú đợt này: (.*)/);
                                if (match) noteText = match[1];
                            }
                            
                            const editBtn = isManager ? `<button class="btn btn-sm btn-link text-warning p-0 float-end" onclick="openNoteEdit('${o.id}', '${noteText.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')"><i class="bi bi-pencil-fill"></i> Sửa</button>` : "";
                            
                            if (!noteText.trim()) {
                                return isManager ? `<div class="mt-2 mb-3"><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-warning w-100" onclick="openNoteEdit('${o.id}', '')"><i class="bi bi-plus-circle"></i> Thêm lưu ý cho đơn</button></div>` : "";
                            }
                            
                            return `<div class="mt-2 mb-3 p-3 rounded shadow-sm position-relative" style="background: #fff3cd; color: #856404; border: 2px solid #ffeeba; border-left: 8px solid #ffc107; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.4;">
                                ${editBtn}
                                <div class="fw-bold mb-1"><i class="bi bi-exclamation-triangle-fill"></i> LƯU Ý QUAN TRỌNG:</div>
                                <div class="fw-bold fs-5">${noteText}</div>
                            </div>`;
                        })()}

                        <div class="progress-grid">
                            <div class="progress-item ${window.autoStage === 'Cắt' ? 'active shadow-sm border-danger' : ''}"><div class="progress-label">✂️ Cắt</div><div class="progress-val">${o.progressDetail["Cắt"] || 0}/${o.qty}</div></div>
                            <div class="progress-item ${window.autoStage === 'May' ? 'active shadow-sm border-primary' : ''}"><div class="progress-label">🧵 May</div><div class="progress-val">${o.progressDetail["May"] || 0}/${o.qty}</div></div>
                            <div class="progress-item ${window.autoStage === 'Khâu tay' ? 'active shadow-sm border-dark' : ''}"><div class="progress-label">🪡 Khâu tay</div><div class="progress-val">${o.progressDetail["Khâu tay"] || 0}/${o.qty}</div></div>
                            <div class="progress-item ${window.autoStage === 'Bơm' ? 'active shadow-sm border-info' : ''}"><div class="progress-label">☁️ Bơm</div><div class="progress-val">${o.progressDetail["Bơm"] || 0}/${o.qty}</div></div>
                            <div class="progress-item ${window.autoStage === 'Đóng gói (đóng bao/dán mắt)' ? 'active shadow-sm border-info' : ''}"><div class="progress-label">📦 Đóng gói (bao/mắt)</div><div class="progress-val">${o.progressDetail["Đóng gói (đóng bao/dán mắt)"] || 0}/${o.qty}</div></div>
                            <div class="progress-item ${(!window.autoStage || window.autoStage === 'Hoàn thiện' || window.autoStage === '📦 Đóng gói') ? 'active shadow-sm border-success' : ''}" style="grid-column: span 2; background: #f0fdf4;">
                                <div class="progress-label text-success">📦 Hoàn thiện (KCS/Nhập kho)</div>
                                <div class="progress-val done text-success">${o.done}/${o.qty}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <label class="small fw-bold text-muted mb-1">Cập nhật số lượng:</label>
                        <div class="qty-control-group">
                            <button class="btn-qty" onclick="adjQ('${o.id}', -1, ${remaining})"><i class="bi bi-dash"></i></button>
                            <input type="number" id="q-${o.id}" class="form-control input-qty-lg" value="" placeholder="Nhập SL">
                            <button class="btn-qty" onclick="adjQ('${o.id}', 1, ${remaining})"><i class="bi bi-plus"></i></button>
                        </div>
                        <div class="quick-actions">
                            <span class="badge bg-secondary badge-action" onclick="adjQ('${o.id}', 5, ${remaining})">+5</span>
                            <span class="badge bg-secondary badge-action" onclick="adjQ('${o.id}', 20, ${remaining})">+20</span>
                            <span class="badge bg-primary badge-action" onclick="setQ('${o.id}', ${remaining})">Tất cả (${remaining})</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="input-group input-group-sm mt-3">
                            <span class="input-group-text bg-white border-end-0"><i class="bi bi-pencil"></i></span>
                            <input type="text" id="n-${o.id}" class="form-control border-start-0" placeholder="Ghi chú SX...">
                            <button class="btn btn-outline-secondary" onclick="showQrCode('${qrUrl}', '${o.id}', '${o.name}', '${finalImgSrc}')"><i class="bi bi-qr-code"></i></button>
                        </div>
                        <div class="progress mt-3" style="height: 6px;">
                            <div class="progress-bar bg-success" style="width:${pct}%"></div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-end small mt-1 text-muted">${pct}% hoàn thành</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>`;
            });
            h += '</div><div style="height: 80px;"></div>'; c.innerHTML = h;
        }

        function syncCalendar() {
            const btn = event.target.closest('button');
            const oldHtml = btn.innerHTML;
            btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Đang đồng bộ...';
            btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                showMsg(res);

            }).syncActiveOrdersToCalendar();
        }
        function saveAllProgress() {
            const container = document.getElementById('ol'); const cards = container.getElementsByClassName('card-custom'); if (cards.length === 0) return;
            const btn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="saveAllProgress()"]'); const oldText = btn.innerHTML; let updates = [];
            for (let card of cards) { const qtyInput = card.querySelector('.input-qty-lg'); const noteInput = card.querySelector('input[type="text"]'); if (qtyInput && noteInput) { updates.push({ id: qtyInput.id.replace('q-', ""), done: qtyInput.value, note: noteInput.value, status: "" }); } }
            if (updates.length === 0) return;
            const validUpdates = [];
            for (let update of updates) {
                if (update.done && update.done > 0) {
                    const card = [...cards].find(c => c.querySelector('.input-qty-lg').id === 'q-' + update.id);
                    const actionBtn = card.querySelector('.badge-action[onclick*="setQ"]');
                    const max = actionBtn ? (parseInt(actionBtn.innerText.match(/\d+/)[0]) || 0) : 0;
                    if (parseInt(update.done) > max) {
                        showMsg("Đơn #" + update.id + ": Số lượng " + update.done + " vượt quá số lượng còn lại (" + max + ")!", 'warning');
                        return;
                    }
                    validUpdates.push(update);
                }
            }
            if (validUpdates.length === 0) { showMsg("Chưa nhập số lượng hợp lệ cho đơn nào!", 'info'); return; }
            
            const performUpdate = () => {
                showAsk("Cập nhật tiến độ " + validUpdates.length + " đơn hàng?", () => {
                    btn.innerHTML = "..."; btn.disabled = true; 
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { 
                        showMsg(res); 
                        btn.innerHTML = oldText; btn.disabled = false; 
                        loadProductionData(); 
                    }).batchUpdateProduction(validUpdates);
                });
            };

            // CẢNH BÁO NẾU CÔNG NHÂN MAY/CẮT... ĐANG NHẬP VÀO Ô MẶC ĐỊNH (HOÀN THIỆN)
            if (!window.autoStage || window.autoStage === 'Hoàn thiện' || window.autoStage === '📦 Đóng gói') {
                showAsk("⚠️ BẠN ĐANG CẬP NHẬT GIAI ĐOẠN 'Hoàn thiện (KCS/Nhập kho)'.\n\nXác nhận đây là bước cuối cùng của đơn hàng?", performUpdate);
            } else {
                performUpdate();
            }
        }

        function openScanModal() { new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('qrScanModal')).show(); if (window.autoStage) { document.getElementById('pStage').value = window.autoStage; } resetScanner(); }
        function resetScanner() { document.getElementById('reader').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('progressForm').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('start-scan-btn').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('qr-result').style.display = 'none'; if (html5QrcodeScanner) { try { html5QrcodeScanner.stop(); } catch (e) { } } }
        function startQRScanner() { document.getElementById('start-scan-btn').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('reader').style.display = 'block'; html5QrcodeScanner = new Html5Qrcode("reader"); html5QrcodeScanner.start({ facingMode: "environment" }, { fps: 10, qrbox: { width: 250, height: 250 } }, onScanSuccess); }
        function onScanSuccess(decodedText, decodedResult) { html5QrcodeScanner.stop().then((ignore) => { try { const data = JSON.parse(decodedText); if (data.id && data.product) { document.getElementById('reader').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('progressForm').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('pOrderId').value = data.id; document.getElementById('pProductName').value = data.product; document.getElementById('scan-msg').innerText = "Đã quét: Đơn #" + data.id; document.getElementById('qr-result').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('pQty').focus(); } else { showMsg("Mã QR không hợp lệ!", 'error'); resetScanner(); } } catch (e) { showMsg("Lỗi đọc mã QR: " + decodedText, 'error'); resetScanner(); } }); }
        function submitProgress() {
            const id = document.getElementById('pOrderId').value; 
            const stage = document.getElementById('pStage').value; 
            const qty = document.getElementById('pQty').value; 
            const defectQty = document.getElementById('pDefect').value || 0;
            const worker = document.getElementById('pWorker').value; 
            const img = document.getElementById('pImgId').value; 
            const price = document.getElementById('pPrice').value;
            
            if (!qty || qty <= 0) { showMsg("Vui lòng nhập số lượng!", 'warning'); return; } 
            if (!worker) { showMsg("Vui lòng chọn thợ!", 'warning'); return; } 
            if (!img) { showMsg("BẮT BUỘC: Phải chụp ảnh sản phẩm!", 'error'); return; }
            
            const doSubmit = () => {
                const btn = event.target; const oldText = btn.innerText; btn.innerText = "Đang lưu..."; btn.disabled = true;
                const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; 
                const imgName = "TIENDO_" + worker + "_" + id + "_" + today + ".jpg";
                const data = { id: id, stage: stage, qty: qty, defectQty: defectQty, price: price, worker: worker, imgData: img, imgName: imgName };
                
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { 
                    showMsg(res); 
                    btn.innerText = oldText; btn.disabled = false; 
                    document.getElementById('pImgId').value = ""; 
                    document.getElementById('pImgPreview').style.display = "none"; 
                    document.getElementById('pPrice').value = ""; 
                    document.getElementById('pDefect').value = ""; 
                    bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('qrScanModal')).hide(); 
                    loadProductionData(); 
                }).submitStageProgress(data);
            };

            if (stage === 'Hoàn thiện' || stage.includes('Đóng gói')) {
                showAsk("⚠️ Bạn đang nộp 'Hoàn thiện (KCS/Nhập kho)'.\n\nXác nhận đây là bước cuối cùng?", doSubmit);
            } else {
                doSubmit();
            }
        }

        function submitPay() {
            const btn = event.target; const img = document.getElementById('payImgId').value;
            const worker = document.getElementById('payWorker').value; const dateVal = document.getElementById('payDate').value; const soVal = document.getElementById('paySO').value; const price = document.getElementById('payPrice').value; const qty = document.getElementById('payQty').value;
            if (!worker || !dateVal || !qty || !price) return showMsg("Vui lòng điền đủ thông tin!", 'warning');

            const doSubmit = () => {
                const fileName = "PhieuGiaCong_" + removeVietnameseTones(worker) + "_" + dateVal + ".jpg"; btn.innerText = "..."; btn.disabled = true;
                const data = { date: dateVal, worker: worker, stage: document.getElementById('payStage').value, product: document.getElementById('payProduct').value, so: soVal, qty: qty, price: price, total: document.getElementById('payTotal').value, imgData: img, imgName: fileName, note: document.getElementById('payNote').value };
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { showMsg(res); btn.innerText = "LƯU NGHIỆM THU"; btn.disabled = false; $('#payProduct').val("").trigger('change'); document.getElementById('payQty').value = ""; document.getElementById('payPrice').value = ""; document.getElementById('payTotal').value = "0"; document.getElementById('payImgId').value = ""; document.getElementById('payImgPreview').style.display = "none"; document.getElementById('paySO').value = ""; loadPayrollData(); }).submitPayroll(data);
            };

            if (!img) {
                showAsk("Chưa có ảnh chứng từ. Vẫn lưu?", doSubmit);
            } else {
                doSubmit();
            }
        }

        function filterPayroll() { const s = document.getElementById('payStart').value; const e = document.getElementById('payEnd').value; if (!s || !e) { showMsg("Chọn ngày bắt đầu/kết thúc!", 'info'); return; } document.getElementById('payrollHistory').innerHTML = "<div class='text-center py-2'>Đang tính toán...</div>"; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => { showPayHistory(data.list); const tDiv = document.getElementById('payrollTotal'); tDiv.innerHTML = "Tổng lương: <span class=\"text-danger fs-5\">" + data.total + " VNĐ</span>"; tDiv.style.display = "block"; }).getPayrollFiltered(s, e); }
        // --- CẬP NHẬT: Thêm cột checkbox chọn in ---
        // --- CẬP NHẬT: Bỏ cột Duyệt, Tách cột Xóa riêng ---
        function showPayHistory(data) {
            const div = document.getElementById('payrollHistory');
            if (!data || data.length === 0) {
                div.innerHTML = "<p class='text-muted text-center pt-3'>Chưa có dữ liệu.</p>"; return;
            }

            let html = '<table class="table table-custom align-middle"><thead><tr>';

            // Cột 1: Checkbox chọn in PDF
            html += '<th style="width:40px" class="text-center"><input type="checkbox" onchange="toggleAllPrint(this)"></th>';

            // Các cột thông tin
            html += '<th>Ngày</th><th>Thợ</th><th>Công đoạn & SP</th><th>Tiền</th><th>Ảnh</th>';

            // Cột cuối: Xóa
            html += '<th style="width:50px" class="text-center">Xóa</th></tr></thead><tbody>';

            data.forEach(r => {
                let link = r.img ? "<a href=\"" + r.img + "\" target=\"_blank\">Xem</a>" : "";

                // Kiểm tra quyền: Worker (Thợ) và Shipper KHÔNG ĐƯỢC xóa
                // Chỉ Admin/Sale/Xưởng trưởng mới thấy nút xóa
                let allowDelete = (window.currentRole !== 'worker' && window.currentRole !== 'shipper');

                // Checkbox chọn in (Cột 1)
                let printCheckHtml = `<input type="checkbox" class="form-check-input chk-print border-primary" value="${r.id}">`;

                // Nút xóa (Cột cuối)
                let deleteHtml = "";
                if (allowDelete) {
                    deleteHtml = `<button class="btn btn-sm text-danger border-0" onclick="deletePayItem('${r.id}', this)" title="Xóa dòng này"><i class="bi bi-trash-fill fs-6"></i></button>`;
                }

                html += "<tr>";
                html += "<td class='text-center'>" + printCheckHtml + "</td>";
                html += "<td>" + r.date + "</td>";
                html += "<td>" + r.worker + "</td>";
                html += "<td>" + r.stage + " - <span class='fw-bold'>" + r.product + "</span><br><small class='text-muted'>SL: " + r.qty + "</small></td>";
                html += "<td class=\"fw-bold\">" + r.total + "</td>";
                html += "<td class=\"text-center\">" + link + "</td>";
                html += "<td class='text-center'>" + deleteHtml + "</td>";
                html += "</tr>";
            });
            html += "</tbody></table>"; div.innerHTML = html;
        }

        }

        function loadShipperData() { document.getElementById('sl').innerHTML = ""; document.getElementById('ls').style.display = "block"; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(rS).getShipperOrders(); }
        function rS(os) {
            document.getElementById('ls').style.display = "none"; const c = document.getElementById('sl');
            if (os.length === 0) { c.innerHTML = "<div class='col-12 text-center py-5 text-muted'>Hết đơn chờ giao! (Hoặc chưa có hàng SX xong)</div>"; return; }
            let h = "";
            os.forEach(o => {
                let rawImg = getSafeImgUrl(o.image);
                let imgDisplay = (rawImg) ? `<div class="img-thumb-container"><img src="${rawImg}=s800" class="img-thumb" onclick="sl('${rawImg}=s3000')"></div>` : '<div class="bg-light rounded mb-3 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center border text-muted" style="height: 150px;">Chưa có ảnh</div>';
                h += `<div class="col-md-6 col-lg-4"><div class="card-custom h-100" id="c-${o.id}"><div class="card-body-custom">${imgDisplay}<div class="d-flex justify-content-between mb-2"><h5 class="fw-bold text-success mb-0 text-truncate">${o.product}</h5><span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">#${o.id}</span></div><div class="mb-1 text-muted small"><i class="bi bi-person"></i> ${o.customer}</div><div class="mb-1 text-dark small"><i class="bi bi-geo-alt-fill text-danger"></i> ${o.address || "Chưa có địa chỉ"}</div><div class="mb-2 text-primary small fw-bold"><i class="bi bi-telephone-fill"></i> ${o.phone || "Chưa có SĐT"}</div><div class="alert alert-warning border small p-2 mb-2"><div class="d-flex justify-content-between"><span>Đã SX:</span><b>${o.doneQty}</b></div><div class="d-flex justify-content-between"><span>Đã Giao:</span><b>${o.shippedQty}</b></div><hr class="my-1"><div class="d-flex justify-content-between fw-bold text-danger"><span>SẴN SÀNG GIAO:</span> <span class="fs-6">${o.readyToShip}</span></div></div><div class="mb-3"><label class="small fw-bold mb-1">Số lượng giao đợt này:</label><input type="number" id="sq-${o.id}" class="form-control fw-bold border-success text-success" max="${o.readyToShip}" value="${o.readyToShip}"></div><div class="mb-3"><input type="file" id="cam-${o.id}" accept="image/*" capture="camera" hidden onchange="rs('cam-${o.id}','d-${o.id}')"><input type="hidden" id="d-${o.id}"><label for="cam-${o.id}" class="btn-camera text-center py-2 w-100"><i class="bi bi-camera"></i> Chụp POD</label></div><button class="btn btn-success w-100 fw-bold py-2 shadow-sm" onclick="fD('${o.id}')">XÁC NHẬN GIAO HÀNG</button></div></div></div>`;
            });
            c.innerHTML = h;
        }
        async function fD(id) { const q = document.getElementById("sq-" + id).value; const img = document.getElementById("d-" + id).value; if (!q || q <= 0) { alert("Nhập số lượng!"); return; } if (!img) { alert("Chụp ảnh đi!"); return; } if (!(await showConfirm("Giao " + q + " cái?"))) return; document.getElementById("c-" + id).style.opacity = '0.5'; const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; const fileName = "POD_" + id + "_" + today + ".jpg"; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(r => { alert(r); loadShipperData(); }).submitPartialDelivery(id, q, img, fileName); }
        function removeVietnameseTones(str) { str = str.replace(/à|á|ạ|ả|ã|â|ầ|ấ|ậ|ẩ|ẫ|ă|ằ|ắ|ặ|ẳ|ẵ/g, "a"); str = str.replace(/è|é|ẹ|ẻ|ẽ|ê|ề|ế|ệ|ể|ễ/g, "e"); str = str.replace(/ì|í|ị|ỉ|ĩ/g, "i"); str = str.replace(/ò|ó|ọ|ỏ|õ|ô|ồ|ố|ộ|ổ|ỗ|ơ|ờ|ớ|ợ|ở|ỡ/g, "o"); str = str.replace(/ù|ú|ụ|ủ|ũ|ư|ừ|ứ|ự|ử|ữ/g, "u"); str = str.replace(/ỳ|ý|ỵ|ỷ|ỹ/g, "y"); str = str.replace(/đ/g, "d"); return str.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, "_"); }
        function rs(i, h, p) { const f = document.getElementById(i).files[0]; if (!f) return; const r = new FileReader(); r.onload = function (e) { const g = new Image(); g.onload = function () { const c = document.createElement('canvas'), x = c.getContext('2d'), M = 800; let w = g.width, t = g.height; if (w > M) { t *= M / w; w = M; } c.width = w; c.height = t; x.drawImage(g, 0, 0, w, t); document.getElementById(h).value = c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.7); if (document.getElementById('in')) document.getElementById('in').value = f.name; if (p) { const z = document.getElementById(p); z.src = c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.7); z.style.display = 'block'; } if (i.startsWith('cam-')) document.querySelector("label[for='" + i + "']").classList.add('has-img'); }; g.src = e.target.result; }; r.readAsDataURL(f); }
        function loadDashboard() {
            document.getElementById('loadDash').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('dashContent').style.display = 'none';

            const isExec = (window.currentRole === 'ceo' || window.currentRole === 'acc');
            const isManager = (isExec || window.currentRole === 'sale' || window.currentRole === 'prod');

            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                rD(res);
                if (isExec) {
                    renderExecutiveDashboard(res);
                    if (res.stratIntel) {
                        document.getElementById('strat-intel-section').style.display = 'block';
                        renderStrategicIntelligence(res.stratIntel);
                    }
                }
                if (isManager) {
                    document.getElementById('prod-intel-section').style.display = 'block';
                    if (res.prodIntel) renderProductionIntelligence(res.prodIntel);
                }
                loadCalendar();
            }).getDashboardData(isManager, isExec, isExec); // (wantProd, wantExec, wantStrategic)
        }

        function rD(d) {
            document.getElementById('loadDash').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('dashContent').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('dash-orders').innerText = d.totalOrders;
            document.getElementById('dash-done').innerText = d.doneQty;
            document.getElementById('dash-total').innerText = d.totalQty;

            const rs = document.getElementById('risk-section');
            const rb = document.getElementById('risk-table-body');

            if (window.currentRole === 'ceo' || window.currentRole === 'acc') {
                rs.style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                if (!d.riskList || d.riskList.length === 0) {
                    rs.style.display = 'none';
                } else {
                    rs.style.display = 'block';
                    rb.innerHTML = d.riskList.map(i => "<tr><td class=\"fw-bold text-danger\">#" + i.id + "</td><td>" + i.customer + "</td><td><div class=\"progress\" style=\"height:6px;width:100px\"><div class=\"progress-bar bg-danger\" style=\"width:" + i.percent + "%\"></div></div></td><td class=\"text-danger small fw-bold\">Còn " + i.daysLeft + " ngày</td></tr>").join("");
                }
            }
        }

        function renderExecutiveDashboard(data) {
            if (!data.execData) return;
            const ed = data.execData;
            window.latestTargetData = ed.targetData; 
        }

        // --- PRODUCTION INTELLIGENCE RENDERING ---
        function renderProductionIntelligence(data) {
            if (!data) return;
            document.getElementById('prod-intel-section').style.display = 'block';

            // 1. Bottleneck Chart
            const bLabels = data.bottleneck.map(i => i.stage);
            const bValues = data.bottleneck.map(i => i.avgHours);
            
            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-bottleneck"), {
                series: [{ name: 'Giờ trung bình/sản phẩm', data: bValues }],
                chart: { type: 'bar', height: 300, toolbar: { show: false } },
                plotOptions: { bar: { borderRadius: 4, horizontal: true } },
                colors: ['#0dcaf0'],
                xaxis: { categories: bLabels },
                title: { text: 'Thời gian trễ (Giờ)', align: 'center', style: { fontSize: '12px' } }
            }).render();

            // 2. Waste Chart
            const wLabels = data.waste.map(i => i.stage);
            const wRates = data.waste.map(i => i.rate);
            
            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-waste"), {
                series: [{ name: 'Tỷ lệ lỗi (%)', data: wRates }],
                chart: { type: 'line', height: 300, toolbar: { show: false } },
                stroke: { curve: 'smooth', width: 3 },
                colors: ['#dc3545'],
                xaxis: { categories: wLabels },
                markers: { size: 5 },
                title: { text: 'Tỷ lệ phế phẩm (%)', align: 'center', style: { fontSize: '12px' } }
            }).render();

            // 3. Productivity Table
            const tbody = document.getElementById('productivity-table-body');
            if (!data.productivity || data.productivity.length === 0) {
                tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-3">Chưa có dữ liệu sản lượng.</td></tr>';
            } else {
                let html = "";
                const avgTotal = data.productivity.reduce((a, b) => a + b.total, 0) / data.productivity.length;
                data.productivity.forEach((w, idx) => {
                    const diffPerc = ((w.total - avgTotal) / (avgTotal || 1) * 100).toFixed(0);
                    const diffColor = diffPerc >= 0 ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger';
                    const icon = diffPerc >= 0 ? 'bi-arrow-up-short' : 'bi-arrow-down-short';
                    html += `<tr><td><span class="badge ${idx < 3 ? 'bg-warning text-dark' : 'bg-light text-dark border'}">${idx + 1}</span></td><td class="fw-bold">${w.name}</td><td class="text-primary fw-bold">${w.total.toLocaleString()}</td><td class="${diffColor} small fw-bold"><i class="bi ${icon}"></i> ${Math.abs(diffPerc)}% so với TB</td></tr>`;
                });
                tbody.innerHTML = html;
            }

            // 4. Production Trend Chart
            if (data.trend) {
                new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-prod-trend"), {
                    series: [{ name: 'Sản phẩm hoàn thiện', data: data.trend.values }],
                    chart: { type: 'area', height: 300, toolbar: { show: false } },
                    dataLabels: { enabled: false },
                    stroke: { curve: 'smooth', width: 2 },
                    colors: ['#0d6efd'],
                    fill: { type: 'gradient', gradient: { shadeIntensity: 1, opacityFrom: 0.4, opacityTo: 0.1 } },
                    xaxis: { categories: data.trend.labels },
                    title: { text: 'Sản lượng theo ngày', align: 'center', style: { fontSize: '12px' } }
                }).render();
            }

            // 5. Cycle Time Table
            const ctBody = document.getElementById('cycle-time-table-body');
            if (!data.cycleTimes || data.cycleTimes.length === 0) {
                ctBody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="2" class="text-center py-3">Chưa có đủ dữ liệu chu kỳ.</td></tr>';
            } else {
                ctBody.innerHTML = data.cycleTimes.map(i => `<tr><td class="fw-bold text-dark">#${i.id}</td><td class="text-end fw-bold text-warning">${i.hours} h</td></tr>`).join("");
            }
        }

        // --- STRATEGIC INTELLIGENCE RENDERING ---
        function renderStrategicIntelligence(data) {
            if (!data) return;

            const wrap = (s) => {
                if (!s) return "";
                const w = s.split(" ");
                if (w.length <= 3) return s;
                const mid = Math.ceil(w.length / 2);
                return [w.slice(0, mid).join(" "), w.slice(mid).join(" ")];
            };

            // 1. P&L by Product
            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-pl-product"), {
                series: [{ name: 'Lợi nhuận', data: data.finance.plProduct.map(i => i.profit) }],
                chart: { type: 'bar', height: 280, toolbar: { show: false } },
                plotOptions: { 
                    bar: { 
                        distributed: true, borderRadius: 4,
                        dataLabels: { position: 'top' }
                    } 
                },
                dataLabels: {
                    enabled: true,
                    offsetY: -20,
                    style: { fontSize: '12px', colors: ["#304758"] },
                    formatter: function (val) {
                        return (val / 1000000).toFixed(1) + "M";
                    }
                },
                xaxis: { 
                    categories: data.finance.plProduct.map(i => wrap(i.name)),
                    labels: { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 500 } }
                },
                yaxis: {
                    labels: {
                        formatter: function (val) {
                            return (val / 1000000).toFixed(0) + "M";
                        }
                    }
                },
                tooltip: {
                    y: {
                        formatter: function (val) {
                            return val.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " VNĐ";
                        }
                    }
                },
                colors: ['#0d6efd', '#6610f2', '#6f42c1', '#d63384', '#fd7e14'],
                legend: { show: false }
            }).render();

            // 2. P&L by Customer
            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-pl-customer"), {
                series: [{ name: 'Lợi nhuận', data: data.finance.plCustomer.map(i => i.profit) }],
                chart: { type: 'bar', height: 280, toolbar: { show: false } },
                plotOptions: { 
                    bar: { 
                        distributed: true, borderRadius: 4,
                        dataLabels: { position: 'top' }
                    } 
                },
                dataLabels: {
                    enabled: true,
                    offsetY: -20,
                    style: { fontSize: '12px', colors: ["#304758"] },
                    formatter: function (val) {
                        return (val / 1000000).toFixed(1) + "M";
                    }
                },
                xaxis: { 
                    categories: data.finance.plCustomer.map(i => wrap(i.name)),
                    labels: { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 500 } }
                },
                yaxis: {
                    labels: {
                        formatter: function (val) {
                            return (val / 1000000).toFixed(0) + "M";
                        }
                    }
                },
                tooltip: {
                    y: {
                        formatter: function (val) {
                            return val.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " VNĐ";
                        }
                    }
                },
                colors: ['#20c997', '#198754', '#ffc107', '#dc3545', '#0dcaf0'],
                legend: { show: false }
            }).render();

            // 3. RFM Table
            const rfmBody = document.getElementById('rfm-table-body');
            rfmBody.innerHTML = data.sales.rfm.map(i => {
                let status = "Tiềm năng";
                let badge = "bg-info";
                if (i.r < 30 && i.f > 3) { status = "Trung thành"; badge = "bg-success"; }
                else if (i.r > 90) { status = "Cần chú ý"; badge = "bg-danger"; }
                
                return `<tr>
                    <td class="fw-bold">${i.name}</td>
                    <td>${i.r} ngày</td>
                    <td>${i.f} lần</td>
                    <td class="text-primary fw-bold">${i.m.toLocaleString()}</td>
                    <td><span class="badge ${badge}">${status}</span></td>
                </tr>`;
            }).join("");

            // 4. Forecast Gauge (Actual vs Budget)
            let perf = (data.planning.actual / (data.planning.budget || 1) * 100);
            if (isNaN(perf)) perf = 0;
            const perfDisplay = perf.toFixed(1);

            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-forecast-gauge"), {
                series: [Number(perf.toFixed(0))],
                chart: { height: 260, type: 'radialBar' },
                plotOptions: {
                    radialBar: {
                        startAngle: -135,
                        endAngle: 135,
                        hollow: { size: '70%' },
                        track: { background: "#eee", strokeWidth: '100%' },
                        dataLabels: { 
                            name: { show: true, color: '#666', fontSize: '13px', offsetY: -10 }, 
                            value: { show: true, fontSize: '24px', fontWeight: 'bold', offsetY: 5 } 
                        }
                    }
                },
                fill: { type: 'solid', colors: [perf >= 80 ? '#198754' : '#ffc107'] },
                labels: ['Tiến độ năm']
            }).render();
            
            document.getElementById('forecast-status-msg').innerHTML = `<span class="badge ${perf >= 80 ? 'bg-success' : 'bg-warning'} p-2">Đạt ${perfDisplay}% kế hoạch năm</span>`;

            // 5. OTD Gauge
            let otdRate = (data.sales.otd.onTime / ((data.sales.otd.onTime + data.sales.otd.late) || 1) * 100);
            if (isNaN(otdRate)) otdRate = 0;
            
            new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-otd-gauge"), {
                series: [Number(otdRate.toFixed(1))],
                chart: { height: 260, type: 'radialBar' },
                colors: ['#0d6efd'],
                plotOptions: {
                    radialBar: {
                        hollow: { size: '70%' },
                        dataLabels: { 
                            name: { show: true, fontSize: '13px', color: '#666', offsetY: -10 }, 
                            value: { show: true, fontSize: '24px', fontWeight: 'bold', offsetY: 5 } 
                        }
                    }
                },
                labels: ['Đúng hạn (OTD)']
            }).render();
        }

        function renderTrend(id, val, inverted) {
            const el = document.getElementById(id); if (!el) return;
            if (val === 0 || val === undefined) { el.innerHTML = "--"; return; }
            const isUp = val > 0;
            const colorClass = (isUp !== !!inverted) ? "trend-up" : "trend-down";
            const icon = isUp ? "bi-arrow-up-right" : "bi-arrow-down-right";
            el.className = "exec-trend " + colorClass;
            el.innerHTML = `<i class="bi ${icon}"></i> ${Math.abs(val)}% so tháng trước`;
        }
        
        // --- ApexCharts Implementations ---
        window.apexRevChart = null;
        window.apexCostChart = null;

        function renderApexLineChart(data) {
            // Check library
            if (typeof ApexCharts === 'undefined') { console.error("ApexCharts not loaded"); return; }
            
            // Hủy chart cũ nếu có để vẽ lại
            if (window.apexRevChart) window.apexRevChart.destroy();

            var options = {
                series: [{
                    name: 'Đã hoàn thành',
                    type: 'column',
                    data: data.revenue
                }, {
                    name: 'Mục tiêu (Kế hoạch)',
                    type: 'line',
                    data: data.target
                }],
                chart: {
                    height: 350,
                    type: 'line',
                    fontFamily: 'Inter, sans-serif',
                    toolbar: { show: false }
                },
                stroke: { width: [0, 4], curve: 'smooth' },
                plotOptions: {
                    bar: { borderRadius: 4, columnWidth: '50%' }
                },
                dataLabels: { enabled: false },
                labels: data.labels,
                colors: ['#3b82f6', '#ef4444'], // Blue for actual, Red for target
                xaxis: { type: 'category' },
                yaxis: [{
                    title: { text: 'Doanh thu (VND)' },
                    labels: {
                        formatter: function (value) {
                            if (value >= 1000000) return (value / 1000000).toFixed(0) + " Tr";
                            return value.toLocaleString();
                        }
                    }
                }],
                legend: { position: 'bottom' }
            };

            window.apexRevChart = new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-revenue"), options);
