            window.apexRevChart.render();
        }

        function renderApexPieChart(data) {
             // Check library
             if (typeof ApexCharts === 'undefined') { return; }
             if (window.apexCostChart) window.apexCostChart.destroy();
             
             // Data processing
             const labels = ['Vật tư', 'Nhân công', 'Vận hành', 'Khác'];
             const values = [data.material || 0, data.labor || 0, data.ops || 0, data.other || 0];

             var options = {
                series: values,
                labels: labels,
                chart: {
                    type: 'donut',
                    height: 350,
                    fontFamily: 'Inter, sans-serif',
                    toolbar: { show: false }
                },
                colors: ['#3b82f6', '#10b981', '#f59e0b', '#ef4444'],
                plotOptions: {
                    pie: {
                        donut: {
                            labels: {
                                show: true,
                                total: {
                                    show: true,
                                    label: 'Tổng Chi Phí',
                                    formatter: function (w) {
                                        const t = w.globals.seriesTotals.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                                        return (t / 1000000).toFixed(1) + " Tr";
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                },
                legend: { position: 'bottom' }
            };

            window.apexCostChart = new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chart-cost-structure"), options);
            window.apexCostChart.render();
        }
        // --- JS CHO PHẦN KẾ TOÁN & CHI PHÍ ---
        // --- [MỚI] JS CHO THIẾT LẬP MỤC TIÊU ---
        function openTargetModal() {
            // Updated: Fallback gracefully if no data yet (don't block user, just show empty)
            const d = window.latestTargetData || {}; 
            
            // Helper to safe set
            const setVal = (id, val) => { document.getElementById(id).value = val || 0; };
            
            // Set values if data exists, otherwise default 0
            setVal('t-q1', d.q1 ? d.q1.targetRev : 0); setVal('t-q1-qty', d.q1 ? d.q1.targetQty : 0);
            setVal('t-q2', d.q2 ? d.q2.targetRev : 0); setVal('t-q2-qty', d.q2 ? d.q2.targetQty : 0);
            setVal('t-q3', d.q3 ? d.q3.targetRev : 0); setVal('t-q3-qty', d.q3 ? d.q3.targetQty : 0);
            setVal('t-q4', d.q4 ? d.q4.targetRev : 0); setVal('t-q4-qty', d.q4 ? d.q4.targetQty : 0);
            
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('targetModal')).show();
        }

        function saveTargetsAction(e) {
            const data = {
                q1Rev: document.getElementById('t-q1').value, q1Qty: document.getElementById('t-q1-qty').value,
                q2Rev: document.getElementById('t-q2').value, q2Qty: document.getElementById('t-q2-qty').value,
                q3Rev: document.getElementById('t-q3').value, q3Qty: document.getElementById('t-q3-qty').value,
                q4Rev: document.getElementById('t-q4').value, q4Qty: document.getElementById('t-q4-qty').value
            };
            const btn = e ? e.target : event.target; 
            const oldText = btn.innerText;
            btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "Đang lưu...";
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                alert(res); 
                btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = oldText;
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('targetModal')).hide();
                loadDashboard(); // Reload to refresh charts
            }).saveTargets(data);
        }

        function loadFinanceOverview() {
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                if (data.error) return;
                document.getElementById('fin-balance').innerText = data.balance;
                const tbody = document.getElementById('financeHistory');
                let html = "";
                data.history.forEach(r => {
                    let color = r.type === 'Thu' ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger';
                    let sign = r.type === 'Thu' ? '+' : '-';
                    html += `<tr><td>${r.date}</td><td><span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">${r.id}</span></td><td><div class="text-truncate" style="max-width:150px" title="${r.target}">${r.target}</div></td><td><span class="fw-bold ${color}">${r.type}</span></td><td class="fw-bold ${color}">${sign} ${r.amount}</td></tr>`;
                });
                tbody.innerHTML = html;
            }).getFinanceOverview();
        }
        function openExpenseModal() { new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('expenseModal')).show(); }
        async function submitExpense() {
            const cat = document.getElementById('expCategory').value; const amt = document.getElementById('expAmount').value;
            if (!amt || amt <= 0) return alert("Nhập số tiền hợp lệ!"); if (!(await showConfirm("Xác nhận chi " + Number(amt).toLocaleString() + " đ cho " + cat + "?"))) return;
            const btn = event.target; const oldText = btn.innerText; btn.innerText = "Đang lưu..."; btn.disabled = true;
            const data = { category: cat, amount: amt, method: document.getElementById('expMethod').value, note: document.getElementById('expNote').value };
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { alert(res); btn.innerText = oldText; btn.disabled = false; document.getElementById('expAmount').value = ""; document.getElementById('expNote').value = ""; bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('expenseModal')).hide(); loadFinanceOverview(); }).submitExpense(data);
        }
        function openIncomeModal() { new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('incomeModal')).show(); }
        async function submitGeneralIncome() {
            const cat = document.getElementById('incCategory').value; const amt = document.getElementById('incAmount').value;
            if (!amt || amt <= 0) return alert("Nhập số tiền hợp lệ!"); if (!(await showConfirm("Xác nhận thu " + Number(amt).toLocaleString() + " đ (" + cat + ")?"))) return;
            const btn = event.target; const oldText = btn.innerText; btn.innerText = "Đang lưu..."; btn.disabled = true;
            const data = { category: cat, amount: amt, method: document.getElementById('incMethod').value, note: document.getElementById('incNote').value };
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { alert(res); btn.innerText = oldText; btn.disabled = false; document.getElementById('incAmount').value = ""; document.getElementById('incNote').value = ""; bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('incomeModal')).hide(); loadFinanceOverview(); }).submitGeneralIncome(data);
        }
        function renderSupDebt(data) {
            document.getElementById('st-payable').innerText = data.totalDebt;
            const div = document.getElementById('supDebtList');
            if (data.list.length === 0) { div.innerHTML = "<div class='text-center py-3 text-muted'>Không có nợ NCC.</div>"; return; }
            let html = "";
            data.list.forEach(item => {
                html += `<div class="card-custom border-start border-4 border-danger mb-2"><div class="card-body-custom py-2"><div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center"><div class="fw-bold text-dark">${item.name}</div><span class="badge bg-danger rounded-pill">${item.remain.toLocaleString('vi-VN')}</span></div><div class="small text-muted mt-1"><div>Đã nhập: ${item.imported.toLocaleString('vi-VN')}</div><div>Đã trả: ${item.paid.toLocaleString('vi-VN')}</div></div><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger w-100 mt-2 fw-bold" onclick="openPaySupModal('${item.name}', ${item.remain})">Thanh toán</button></div></div>`;
            });
            div.innerHTML = html;
        }
        function openPaySupModal(name, debt) {
            document.getElementById('psName').innerText = name; 
            document.getElementById('psDebt').innerText = debt.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " đ"; 
            document.getElementById('psAmount').value = debt; 
            document.getElementById('psNote').value = ""; 
            const poSelect = document.getElementById('psPO');
            poSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Đang tải... --</option>';
            poSelect.disabled = true;
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                poSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Chọn Đơn hàng (Không bắt buộc) --</option>';
                if (list && list.length > 0) {
                    list.forEach(po => {
                        poSelect.add(new Option(`Đơn ${po.id} - ${Number(po.total).toLocaleString()} ₫ (${po.status})`, po.id));
                    });
                } else {
                    poSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Không có đơn nợ --</option>';
                }
                poSelect.disabled = false;
            }).getSupplierPOs(name);
            
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('paySupModal')).show();
        }
        async function submitPaySup() {
            const name = document.getElementById('psName').innerText; const amt = document.getElementById('psAmount').value; const method = document.getElementById('psMethod').value; const note = document.getElementById('psNote').value; const poId = document.getElementById('psPO').value;
            if (!amt || amt <= 0) return alert("Nhập số tiền!");

            let confirmMsg = "Xác nhận trả " + Number(amt).toLocaleString() + " đ cho " + name + "?";
            if (poId) confirmMsg = "Xác nhận thanh toán cho ĐƠN " + poId + " (" + Number(amt).toLocaleString() + " đ)?";

            if (!(await showConfirm(confirmMsg))) return;
            const btn = event.target;
            btn.innerText = "Đang xử lý...";
            btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                alert(res);
                btn.innerText = "XÁC NHẬN TRẢ TIỀN";
                btn.disabled = false;
                document.getElementById('psAmount').value = ""; document.getElementById('psNote').value = ""; $('#psPO').val(null).trigger('change');
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('paySupModal')).hide();

                loadAccData(); // Tải lại dữ liệu kế toán
                loadPOList();  // Tải lại danh sách PO (để thấy trạng thái Đã thanh toán)
            }).paySupplier(name, amt, method, note, poId);
        }
        function viewPnL() {
            const m = document.getElementById('pnlMonth').value; const y = document.getElementById('pnlYear').value; const btn = event.target; const oldText = btn.innerText; btn.innerText = "..."; btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                btn.innerText = oldText; btn.disabled = false; document.getElementById('pnlContent').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('pnl-revenue').innerText = res.revenue; document.getElementById('pnl-cogs').innerText = res.cogs; document.getElementById('pnl-gross').innerText = res.grossProfit; document.getElementById('pnl-opex').innerText = res.opex;
                const netEl = document.getElementById('pnl-net'); netEl.innerText = res.netProfit; netEl.className = res.isProfit ? "text-success" : "text-danger";
                let html = ""; for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(res.details)) { html += `<li class="d-flex justify-content-between mb-1"><span>${key}</span><span>${val.toLocaleString('vi-VN')}</span></li>`; }
                document.getElementById('pnl-details').innerHTML = html || "<li class='text-muted'>Không có chi phí khác.</li>";
            }).getPnLReport(m, y);
        }

        // --- JS CHO MODULE MUA HÀNG & PO ---
        function loadPOTab() {
            loadPOList();
            loadPendingRequests(); // Load thêm danh sách yêu cầu
            const sSelect = document.getElementById('poSupplierNew'); sSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Chọn NCC --</option>';
            if (window.suppliersList) { window.suppliersList.forEach(s => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = s; opt.innerText = s; sSelect.appendChild(opt); }); }
        }
        function runMRPAnalysis() {
            document.getElementById('mrpResult').innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center"><div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-warning"></div> Đang tính toán...</td></tr>'; 
            document.getElementById('actionCreatePO').style.display = 'none';
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                const tb = document.getElementById('mrpResult'); 
                if (list.length === 0) { 
                    tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center text-success py-3"><i class="bi bi-check-circle"></i> Kho đã đủ vật tư! Không cần mua thêm.</td></tr>'; 
                    return; 
                }
                let h = ""; 
                list.forEach((item, index) => { 
                    h += `<tr>
                        <td class="text-center"><input type="checkbox" class="mrp-check" value="${index}" data-name="${item.material}" checked></td>
                        <td><div class="fw-bold text-danger">${item.material}</div><div class="text-muted" style="font-size:11px">Thiếu: ${item.missing.toLocaleString()} ${item.unit}</div></td>
                        <td><div>Tồn: ${item.stock}</div><div>Cần: ${item.demand}</div></td>
                        <td><input type="number" class="form-control form-control-sm border-warning fw-bold text-center mrp-qty" id="buy-qty-${index}" value="${item.suggestion}"></td>
                        <td><input type="text" class="form-control form-control-sm text-center mrp-unit" id="buy-unit-${index}" value="${item.unit}" list="unit-list"></td>
                        <td><input type="number" class="form-control form-control-sm border-success fw-bold text-center mrp-price" id="buy-price-${index}" placeholder="Giá"></td>
                    </tr>`; 
                });
                tb.innerHTML = h; 
                document.getElementById('actionCreatePO').style.display = 'block';
            }).runMRP();
        }
        function toggleAllMRP(source) { const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.mrp-check'); checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = source.checked); }
        async function submitCreatePO() {
            const sup = document.getElementById('poSupplierNew').value; if (!sup) return alert("Vui lòng chọn Nhà cung cấp!");
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.mrp-check:checked'); if (checkboxes.length === 0) return alert("Chưa chọn vật tư nào để mua!");
            let items = []; 
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => { 
                let idx = cb.value; 
                let name = cb.getAttribute('data-name'); 
                let unit = document.getElementById('buy-unit-' + idx).value; 
                let qty = document.getElementById('buy-qty-' + idx).value; 
                let price = document.getElementById('buy-price-' + idx).value || 0;
                items.push({ name: name, unit: unit, qty: qty, price: price }); 
            });
            if (!(await showConfirm("Tạo đơn mua hàng cho " + items.length + " vật tư?"))) return;
            const btn = event.target; btn.innerText = "Đang tạo..."; btn.disabled = true;
            const orderId = document.getElementById('poOrderSelectManual').value;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { 
                alert(res); 
                btn.innerText = "TẠO ĐƠN MUA (PO)"; 
                btn.disabled = false; 
                document.getElementById('poSupplierNew').value = ""; 
                document.getElementById('poOrderSelectManual').value = "";
                document.getElementById('mrpResult').innerHTML = ""; 
                document.getElementById('actionCreatePO').style.display = 'none'; 
                loadPOList(); 
            }).createPurchaseOrder({ supplier: sup, items: items, orderId: orderId });
        }
        function loadPOList() {
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_po');
            if (cached) renderPOList(JSON.parse(cached));

            document.getElementById('poList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-3">Đang tải...</div>';
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_po', JSON.stringify(list));
                renderPOList(list);
            }).getPOList();
        }
        function renderPOList(list) {
            const div = document.getElementById('poList');
            if (!list || list.length === 0) { div.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-3 text-muted">Chưa có PO nào.</div>'; return; }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(po => {
                const poStr = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(po));
                h += `<div class="list-group-item list-group-item-action cursor-pointer" onclick="viewPO('${poStr}')">
                    <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
                        <h6 class="mb-1 fw-bold text-danger">${po.id}</h6>
                        <small class="text-muted">${po.date}</small>
                    </div>
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                        <span class="fw-bold text-dark small">${po.supplier}</span>
                        <span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">${po.status}</span>
                    </div>
                    ${po.orderId ? `<div class="text-primary small fw-bold mt-1">🛒 Đơn: #${po.orderId}</div>` : ''}
                    <div class="small text-muted mt-1 text-truncate">${po.details}</div>
                </div>`;
            });
            div.innerHTML = h;
        }

        // --- JS CHO MODULE PO DETAIL & REQUESTS ---
        let currentPO = null;
        function viewPO(poStr) {
            const po = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(poStr)); currentPO = po;
            document.getElementById('podId').innerText = po.id; 
            document.getElementById('podStatus').innerText = po.status; 
            document.getElementById('podSup').innerText = po.supplier; 
            document.getElementById('podDate').innerText = po.date; 
            document.getElementById('podTotal').innerText = (Number(po.amount) || 0).toLocaleString();
            
            const ordBox = document.getElementById('podOrderId');
            if (ordBox) {
                if (po.orderId) {
                    ordBox.closest('div').style.display = 'block';
                    ordBox.innerText = "#" + po.orderId;
                } else {
                    ordBox.closest('div').style.display = 'none';
                }
            }
            document.getElementById('podStatusSelect').value = po.status;
            
            const list = document.getElementById('podItems'); 
            list.innerHTML = "";
            const items = po.details.split('\n'); 
            
            items.forEach((line, idx) => { 
                if (line.trim()) { 
                    let parts = line.split('|').map(p => p.trim());
                    // Format: Tên | SL | ĐVT | Đơn giá | Thành tiền
                    if (parts.length >= 4) {
                        let name = parts[0], qty = parts[1], unit = parts[2], price = parts[3];
                        list.innerHTML += `
                        <li class="list-group-item p-2">
                            <div class="fw-bold small mb-1">${name}</div>
                            <div class="row g-2 align-items-center">
                                <div class="col-4">
                                    <div class="input-group input-group-sm">
                                        <input type="number" class="form-control pod-qty" value="${qty}" onchange="recalculatePodTotal()">
                                        <span class="input-group-text">${unit}</span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="col-1 text-center">x</div>
                                <div class="col-7">
                                    <div class="input-group input-group-sm">
                                        <input type="number" class="form-control pod-price" value="${price}" onchange="recalculatePodTotal()">
                                        <span class="input-group-text">đ</span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <input type="hidden" class="pod-name" value="${name}">
                                <input type="hidden" class="pod-unit" value="${unit}">
                            </div>
                        </li>`;
                    } else {
                        list.innerHTML += `<li class="list-group-item small text-muted">${line}</li>`;
                    }
                } 
            });
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('poDetailModal')).show();
        }

        async function updatePOStatusAction() {
            const newStatus = document.getElementById('podStatusSelect').value; 
            if (!currentPO) return;
            
            const items = [];
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#podItems li.list-group-item');
            rows.forEach(row => {
                const qInput = row.querySelector('.pod-qty');
                if (qInput) {
                    items.push({
                        name: row.querySelector('.pod-name').value,
                        qty: qInput.value,
                        unit: row.querySelector('.pod-unit').value,
                        price: row.querySelector('.pod-price').value
                    });
                }
            });

            if (newStatus === "Hủy") {
                if (!(await showConfirm("Bạn có chắc chắn muốn HỦY đơn mua hàng này không?"))) return;
            }

            const btn = event.target; btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "...";
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { 
                Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Thông báo', text:res, timer:2000}); 
                btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "Lưu"; 
                loadPOList(); 
                document.getElementById('podStatus').innerText = newStatus; 
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('poDetailModal')).hide();
            }).updatePOData(currentPO.id, newStatus, items);
        }

        function printPOPDF() {
            if (!currentPO) return;
            const btn = event.target; const oldText = btn.innerHTML; btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Đang tạo...'; btn.disabled = true;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(url => { btn.innerHTML = oldText; btn.disabled = false; if (url) window.open(url, '_blank'); else Swal.fire({icon:'error', title:'Lỗi', text:'Không thể tạo PDF cho PO này!', timer:2500}); }).createPOReport(currentPO.id);
        }

        function copyPOToWarehouse() {
            if (!currentPO) return;
            bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('poDetailModal')).hide();
            const wareTabBtn = document.querySelector('button[data-bs-target="#warehouse"]'); if (wareTabBtn) wareTabBtn.click();
            setTimeout(() => { 
                document.getElementById('whIn').checked = true; 
                toggleWhPrice('Nhập kho'); 
                $('#whSupplier').val(currentPO.supplier).trigger('change'); 
                document.getElementById('whNote').value = "Nhập từ đơn: " + currentPO.id + ". Chi tiết: " + currentPO.details; 
                $('#whMat').select2('open'); 
                Swal.fire({icon:'info', title:'Thông báo', text:'Đã chuyển thông tin PO sang Kho. Vui lòng chọn từng vật tư và nhập số lượng thực nhận!', confirmButtonText:'Đã hiểu'}); 
            }, 500);
        }

        // --- JS CHO MODULE YÊU CẦU MUA HÀNG (REQUEST) ---
        function openGuestRequest() { document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'none'; openRequestModal(); document.getElementById('guestNameSection').style.display = 'block'; window.isGuestMode = true; }
        function closeGuestMode() { if (window.isGuestMode) { document.getElementById('login-overlay').style.display = 'flex'; window.isGuestMode = false; document.getElementById('guestNameSection').style.display = 'none'; } }
        function openRequestModal() {
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('requestModal')).show();
            if (localStorage.getItem('4f_login') && !window.isGuestMode) { document.getElementById('guestNameSection').style.display = 'none'; }
            const select = $('#reqItem');
            if (select.children('option').length <= 1) {
                select.select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', dropdownParent: $('#requestModal'), tags: true });
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => { data.materials.forEach(m => { select.append(new Option(m, m)); }); }).getDropdownData();
            }
        }
        function submitRequest() {
            const item = $('#reqItem').val(); const qty = document.getElementById('reqQty').value; const priority = document.getElementById('reqPriority').value; const note = document.getElementById('reqNote').value;
            let requester = ""; if (window.isGuestMode) { requester = document.getElementById('reqGuestName').value; if (!requester) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu thông tin', text:'Vui lòng nhập tên của bạn trước khi gửi!', timer:2000}); } else { requester = localStorage.getItem('4f_login') || "Nhân viên"; }
            if (!item || !qty) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu thông tin', text:'Vui lòng chọn vật tư và nhập số lượng!', timer:2000});
            const btn = event.target; btn.innerText = "Đang gửi..."; btn.disabled = true;
            const data = { requester: requester, item: item, qty: qty, priority: priority, note: note };
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Thành công!', text:res, timer:2000, showConfirmButton:false});
                btn.innerText = "GỬI YÊU CẦU"; btn.disabled = false;
                $('#reqItem').val(null).trigger('change'); document.getElementById('reqQty').value = ""; document.getElementById('reqNote').value = ""; document.getElementById('reqGuestName').value = "";
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('requestModal')).hide();
                if (window.isGuestMode) { closeGuestMode(); } else { if (window.loadPendingRequests) loadPendingRequests(); }
            }).submitMaterialRequest(data);
        }

        function loadPendingRequests() {
            const div = document.getElementById('pendingRequestList'); if (!div) return;
            div.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-2"><span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span></div>';
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                // Reset Select All
                if (document.getElementById('chk-all-req')) document.getElementById('chk-all-req').checked = false;

                // Cập nhật Badge trên Bottom Nav & Sidebar
                const badgeBn = document.getElementById('bn-badge-ware');
                if (badgeBn) {
                    if (list.length > 0) {
                        badgeBn.innerText = list.length;
                        badgeBn.style.display = 'block';
                    } else {
                        badgeBn.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }

                if (list.length === 0) { div.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-3 text-muted small">Không có yêu cầu nào mới.</div>'; return; }
                let h = "";
                list.forEach(r => {
                    const badge = r.priority === 'Gấp' ? '<span class="badge bg-danger">GẤP</span>' : '<span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">Thường</span>';
                    const itemEsc = r.item.replace(/'/g, "\\'");
                    const dataStr = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(r));
                    
                    h += `<div class="list-group-item">
                        <div class="d-flex align-items-start gap-2">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="form-check-input chk-req mt-1" value="${r.id}" data-req='${dataStr}'>
                            <div class="flex-grow-1">
                                <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between align-items-center">
                                    <h6 class="mb-1 fw-bold text-primary">${r.item}</h6>
                                    ${badge}
                                </div>
                                <div class="small fw-bold">SL: ${r.qty} <span class="text-muted fw-normal">| Từ: ${r.requester}</span></div>
                                <div class="small text-muted fst-italic mb-2">${r.note}</div>
                                <div class="d-flex gap-2">
                                    <button class="btn btn-sm btn-success w-100 py-0" onclick="procReq('${r.id}', 'approve', '${itemEsc}', '${r.qty}')"><i class="bi bi-check"></i> Duyệt</button>
                                    <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary w-100 py-0" onclick="procReq('${r.id}', 'reject')"><i class="bi bi-x"></i> Hủy</button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                });
                div.innerHTML = h;
            }).getPendingRequests();
        }

        function toggleAllReq(source) {
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.chk-req');
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = source.checked);
        }

        function openBulkApproveModal() {
            const selected = document.querySelectorAll('.chk-req:checked');
            if (selected.length === 0) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Chưa chọn', text:'Vui lòng chọn ít nhất 1 yêu cầu để gom PO!', timer:2000});
            
            let html = "";
            
            selected.forEach((cb) => {
                const r = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(cb.getAttribute('data-req')));
                const unit = (window.materialUnits && window.materialUnits[r.item]) ? window.materialUnits[r.item] : "";
                
                html += `
                <div class="card mb-2 border-start border-3 border-info">
                    <div class="card-body p-2">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-1">
                            <span class="fw-bold text-primary small">${r.item}</span>
                            <span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">${r.id}</span>
                        </div>
                        <input type="hidden" class="bulk-req-id" value="${r.id}">
                        <input type="hidden" class="bulk-req-item" value="${r.item}">
                        <div class="row g-2">
                            <div class="col-4">
                                <label class="small text-muted">SL duyệt</label>
                                <input type="number" class="form-control form-control-sm bulk-req-qty" value="${r.qty}">
                            </div>
                            <div class="col-3">
                                <label class="small text-muted">ĐVT</label>
                                <input type="text" class="form-control form-control-sm bulk-req-unit" value="${unit}">
                            </div>
                            <div class="col-5">
                                <label class="small text-muted">Đơn giá</label>
                                <input type="number" class="form-control form-control-sm bulk-req-price border-danger" placeholder="Giá...">
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            
            const listDiv = document.getElementById('bulkAppReqList');
            if (listDiv) listDiv.innerHTML = html;
            
            // Populate Supplier select if needed (DropdownData should have suppliers)
            const supSelect = $('#bulkAppReqSup');
            if (supSelect.children('option').length <= 1) {
                supSelect.select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', dropdownParent: $('#bulkApproveModal'), tags: true });
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => { data.suppliers.forEach(s => { supSelect.append(new Option(s, s)); }); }).getDropdownData();
            }

            $('#bulkAppReqSup').val("").trigger('change');
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('bulkApproveModal')).show();
        }

        async function submitBulkApproveReq() {
            const supplier = $('#bulkAppReqSup').val();
            if (!supplier) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu NCC', text:'Vui lòng chọn Nhà Cung Cấp!', timer:2000});
            
            const containers = document.querySelectorAll('#bulkAppReqList .card');
            let items = [];
            let ids = [];
            let missingPrice = false;

            containers.forEach(card => {
                const id = card.querySelector('.bulk-req-id').value;
                const item = card.querySelector('.bulk-req-item').value;
                const qty = card.querySelector('.bulk-req-qty').value;
                const unit = card.querySelector('.bulk-req-unit').value;
                const price = card.querySelector('.bulk-req-price').value;

                if (!price) missingPrice = true;

                ids.push(id);
                items.push({ id: id, item: item, qty: qty, unit: unit, price: price });
            });

            if (missingPrice) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu đơn giá', text:'Vui lòng nhập đơn giá cho tất cả vật tư!', timer:2000});
            
            if (!(await showConfirm(`Xác nhận gom ${ids.length} yêu cầu thành 1 PO cho ${supplier}?`))) return;
            
            const btn = event.target; btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "Đang xử lý...";
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Thành công!', text:res, timer:2000, showConfirmButton:false});
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('bulkApproveModal')).hide();
                loadPendingRequests();
                loadPOList();
                btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "XÁC NHẬN TẠO PO TỔNG";
            }).approveMultipleRequestsToPO({ ids: ids, supplier: supplier, items: items });
        }

        // --- CẬP NHẬT: Hàm xử lý Duyệt yêu cầu -> Tạo PO ---
        async function procReq(id, action, item, qty) {
            if (action === 'reject') {
                if (!(await showConfirm("Hủy bỏ yêu cầu này?"))) return;
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                    loadPendingRequests();
                }).processRequest(id, 'reject'); 
            }
            else if (action === 'approve') {
                document.getElementById('appReqId').value = id;
                document.getElementById('appReqItem').value = item;
                document.getElementById('appReqQty').value = qty;
                document.getElementById('appReqUnit').value = (window.materialUnits && window.materialUnits[item]) ? window.materialUnits[item] : "";
                
                const supSelect = $('#appReqSup');
                if (supSelect.children('option').length <= 1) {
                    supSelect.select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', dropdownParent: $('#approveRequestModal'), tags: true });
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => { data.suppliers.forEach(s => { supSelect.append(new Option(s, s)); }); }).getDropdownData();
                }

                $('#appReqSup').val("").trigger('change');
                document.getElementById('appReqPrice').value = "";
                new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('approveRequestModal')).show();
            }
        }

        function submitApproveReq() {
            const id = document.getElementById('appReqId').value;
            const supplier = $('#appReqSup').val();
            const qty = document.getElementById('appReqQty').value;
            const unit = document.getElementById('appReqUnit').value;
            const price = document.getElementById('appReqPrice').value;
            if (!supplier || !qty || !price) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu thông tin', text:'Vui lòng nhập đầy đủ Nhà Cung Cấp, Số lượng và Đơn giá!', timer:2500});
            const btn = event.target; btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "Đang xử lý...";
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Đã tạo PO!', text:res, timer:2000, showConfirmButton:false});
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('approveRequestModal')).hide();
                loadPendingRequests();
                loadPOList();
                btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "XÁC NHẬN TẠO PO";
            }).approveRequestToPO({ id: id, supplier: supplier, qty: qty, price: price, unit: unit });
        }
        // --- [MỚI] Hàm chọn tất cả checkbox in ---
        function toggleAllPrint(source) {
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.chk-print');
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = source.checked);
        }

        // --- [MỚI] Hàm xuất PDF các dòng đã chọn ---
        function exportSelectedPayPDF() {
            // 1. Lấy danh sách ID đã tích chọn
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.chk-print:checked');
            if (checkboxes.length === 0) {
                Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Chưa chọn dòng', text:'Vui lòng tích chọn ít nhất 1 phiếu lương để xuất PDF!', timer:2500});
                return;
            }

            let selectedIds = [];
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => selectedIds.push(cb.value));

            // 2. Gửi yêu cầu lên server
            const btn = event.target;
            const oldText = btn.innerHTML;
            btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Đang tạo...';
            btn.disabled = true;

            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                btn.innerHTML = oldText;
                btn.disabled = false;

                if (res.error) {
                    alert("Lỗi: " + res.error);
                } else {
                    // Mở file PDF trong tab mới
                    window.open(res.url, '_blank');
                }
            }).createSelectedPayrollReport(selectedIds);
        }
        // --- KHU VỰC XỬ LÝ QR & IN ẤN (ĐÃ CẬP NHẬT GIAO DIỆN) ---
        window.currentQrData = {};

        // Hàm nhận 4 tham số: QR Url, ID, Tên SP, Ảnh SP
        function showQrCode(qrUrl, id, name, prodImg) {
            window.currentQrData = {
                qr: qrUrl,
                id: id,
                name: name,
                img: prodImg // Lưu link ảnh sản phẩm
            };

            // Hiển thị lên Modal xem trước
            document.getElementById('qrDisplayId').innerText = "#" + id;
            document.getElementById('qrDisplayName').innerText = name;
            document.getElementById('qrDisplayImg').src = qrUrl; // Modal chỉ cần hiện QR cho gọn

            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('qrDisplayModal')).show();
        }

        function printOrderQR() {
            var d = window.currentQrData;
            if (!d.qr) return;

            var win = window.open('', 'PrintQR', 'height=700,width=600');

            var html = '<html><head><title>IN TEM LỆNH SX</title>';
            html += '<style>';
            html += 'body { font-family: "Palatino", sans-serif; text-align: center; padding: 10px; margin: 0; }';
            // Khung tem
            html += '.ticket { border: 2px dashed #000; padding: 10px; border-radius: 8px; display: inline-block; width: 320px; }';

            // Cấu hình kích thước chữ theo yêu cầu
            html += '.header { font-size: 14px; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 5px; text-transform: uppercase; }';
            html += '.id-text { font-size: 24px; color: #555; font-weight: bold; margin: 0; }'; /* Mã đơn nhỏ lại */
            html += '.name-text { font-size: 32px; font-weight: 800; line-height: 1.1; margin: 10px 0; color: #000; }'; /* Tên to lên */

            // Cấu hình ảnh
            html += '.qr-container { display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 10px; margin-top: 10px; align-items: center; }';
            html += '.qr-img { width: 140px; height: 140px; display: block; border: 1px solid #ddd; }';
            html += '.prod-img { width: 140px; height: 140px; object-fit: cover; border: 1px solid #ddd; border-radius: 4px; }';
            html += '.note { font-size: 12px; font-style: italic; margin-top: 10px; border-top: 1px solid #ccc; padding-top: 5px;}';
            html += '</style></head>';

            // Quan trọng: Thêm onload để đợi ảnh tải xong mới In
            html += '<body onload="setTimeout(function(){ window.print(); window.close(); }, 1000)">';

            html += '<div class="ticket">';
            html += '<div class="header">Lệnh Sản Xuất 4F</div>';

            // 1. Mã đơn hàng (Nhỏ hơn)
            html += '<div class="id-text">#' + d.id + '</div>';

            // 2. Tên sản phẩm (To hơn, Đậm hơn)
            html += '<div class="name-text">' + d.name + '</div>';

            // 3. Khu vực chứa 2 ảnh: QR và Ảnh sản phẩm
            html += '<div class="qr-container">';
            // Mã QR
            html += '<img src="' + d.qr + '" class="qr-img" alt="QR Code">';
            // Ảnh sản phẩm (Nếu có thì in, không có thì ẩn)
            if (d.img && d.img !== 'undefined' && d.img !== '') {
                html += '<img src="' + d.img + '" class="prod-img" alt="Sản phẩm">';
            }
            html += '</div>';

            html += '<div class="note">Quét mã để cập nhật tiến độ</div>';
            html += '</div>';

            html += '</body></html>';

            win.document.write(html);
            win.document.close();
        }

        // --- JS CHO MODULE HỢP ĐỒNG NGUYÊN TẮC ---
        function loadContractsTab() {
            const cached = localStorage.getItem('4f_cache_contracts');
            if (cached) renderContracts(JSON.parse(cached));

            document.getElementById('lc-contracts').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('contractList').innerHTML = "";
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(data => {
                    localStorage.setItem('4f_cache_contracts', JSON.stringify(data));
                    renderContracts(data);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(err => {
                    document.getElementById('lc-contracts').style.display = 'none';
                    Swal.fire({icon:'error', title:'Lỗi tải hợp đồng', text:err.message || String(err)});
                })
                .getContractsData();
        }
        function renderContracts(list) {
            document.getElementById('lc-contracts').style.display = 'none';
            const container = document.getElementById('contractList');
            if (!list || list.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-12 text-center py-5 text-muted">Chưa có hợp đồng nguyên tắc nào.</div>'; return; }
            let h = "";
            list.forEach(c => {
                let pct = Math.min(100, Math.floor((c.calledOff / c.total) * 100));
                let rawImg = getSafeImgUrl(c.image);
                let imgDisplay = (rawImg) ? `<div class="img-thumb-container mb-3"><img src="${rawImg}=s800" class="img-thumb" onclick="sl('${rawImg}=s3000')"></div>` : '';
                h += `<div class="col-md-6 col-lg-4"><div class="card-custom h-100"><div class="card-body-custom"><div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-2"><h6 class="fw-bold text-primary m-0">#${c.id}</h6><span class="badge ${c.status === 'Đang chạy' ? 'bg-success' : 'bg-secondary'} small">${c.status}</span></div><div class="fw-bold fs-5 mb-0 text-dark">${c.customer}</div><div class="text-muted small mb-3">${c.product}</div>${imgDisplay}<div class="mb-1 d-flex justify-content-between small"><span>Đã lấy: <b>${c.calledOff.toLocaleString()}</b></span><span class="text-muted">Tổng: ${c.total.toLocaleString()}</span></div><div class="progress mb-2" style="height: 8px;"><div class="progress-bar bg-info" style="width: ${pct}%"></div></div><div class="text-end small fw-bold text-info mb-3">${pct}%</div><div class="text-muted small mb-3"><i class="bi bi-calendar-range"></i> ${c.start} - ${c.end}</div><div class="d-grid gap-2"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm fw-bold py-2" onclick="openCallOffModal('${c.id}', '${c.customer}', '${c.product}', ${c.price})"><i class="bi bi-telephone-outbound"></i> GỌI HÀNG (CALL-OFF)</button><button class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm" onclick="openContractModal('${encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(c))}')"><i class="bi bi-pencil"></i> Sửa HĐ</button></div></div></div></div>`;
            });
            container.innerHTML = h;
        }
        function openContractModal(dataStr) {
            const form = document.getElementById('contractForm');
            form.reset();
            document.getElementById('conId').value = "";

            const custSelect = $('#conCustomer');
            const prodSelect = $('#conProduct');
            if (custSelect.children().length <= 1) {
                custSelect.html($('#customerSelect').html());
                prodSelect.html($('#bomProduct').html());
            }

            document.getElementById('conImgData').value = "";
            document.getElementById('conImgPreview').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('conImgPlaceholder').style.display = 'block';

            if (dataStr) {
                const c = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(dataStr));
                document.getElementById('conId').value = c.id;
                custSelect.val(c.customer).trigger('change');
                prodSelect.val(c.product).trigger('change');
                document.getElementById('conTotal').value = c.total;
                document.getElementById('conPrice').value = c.price;
                document.getElementById('conStart').value = c.startRaw ? new Date(c.startRaw).toISOString().split('T')[0] : "";
                document.getElementById('conEnd').value = c.endRaw ? new Date(c.endRaw).toISOString().split('T')[0] : "";
                document.getElementById('conStatus').value = c.status;
                document.getElementById('conNote').value = c.note || "";
                
                if (c.image) {
                   const imgUrl = getSafeImgUrl(c.image);
                   document.getElementById('conImgPreview').src = imgUrl + "=s400";
                   document.getElementById('conImgPreview').style.display = 'block';
                   document.getElementById('conImgPlaceholder').style.display = 'none';
                }
            } else {
                document.getElementById('conStart').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
            }

            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('contractModal')).show();
            setTimeout(() => { 
                $('.select2-con').select2({ 
                    theme: 'bootstrap-5', 
                    dropdownParent: $('#contractModal'),
                    tags: true // Cho phép nhập tay sản phẩm mới
                }); 
            }, 200);
        }
        function submitContractAction() {
            const f = document.getElementById('contractForm');
            if (!f.checkValidity()) { f.reportValidity(); return; }
            const btn = event.target; btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "...";
            const data = {
                id: document.getElementById('conId').value,
                customer: document.getElementById('conCustomer').value,
                product: document.getElementById('conProduct').value,
                total: document.getElementById('conTotal').value,
                price: document.getElementById('conPrice').value,
                start: document.getElementById('conStart').value,
                end: document.getElementById('conEnd').value,
                status: document.getElementById('conStatus').value,
                note: document.getElementById('conNote').value,
                imageData: document.getElementById('conImgData').value,
                imageName: "Contract_" + document.getElementById('conId').value + ".jpg"
            };
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(res => {
                    Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Thành công!', text:res, timer:2000, showConfirmButton:false});
                    btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "LƯU HỢP ĐỒNG";
                    f.reset();
                    bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('contractModal')).hide();
                    loadContractsTab();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(err => {
                    Swal.fire({icon:'error', title:'Lỗi lưu hợp đồng', text:err.message || String(err)});
                    btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "LƯU HỢP ĐỒNG";
                })
                .submitContract(data);
        }
        function openCallOffModal(id, cust, prod, price) {
            document.getElementById('coId').value = id;
            document.getElementById('coIdDisplay').innerText = id;
            document.getElementById('coCustDisplay').innerText = cust;
            document.getElementById('coProdDisplay').innerText = prod;
            document.getElementById('coPriceDisplay').innerText = Number(price).toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " đ";
            document.getElementById('coDate').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
            document.getElementById('coQty').value = "";
            document.getElementById('coNote').value = "";
            document.getElementById('coDeadline').value = "";
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('callOffModal')).show();
        }
        async function submitCallOffAction() {
            const qty = document.getElementById('coQty').value; if (!qty || qty <= 0) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Thiếu thông tin', text:'Vui lòng nhập số lượng gọi hàng!', timer:2000});
            if (!(await showConfirm("Xác nhận tạo lệnh giao hàng " + qty + " cái cho hợp đồng này?"))) return;
            const btn = event.target; btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = "...";
            const data = {
                contractId: document.getElementById('coId').value,
                qty: qty,
                date: document.getElementById('coDate').value,
                deadline: document.getElementById('coDeadline').value,
                note: document.getElementById('coNote').value
            };
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Đã gọi hàng!', text:res, timer:2000, showConfirmButton:false});
                btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = "XÁC NHẬN GỌI HÀNG";
                document.getElementById('coQty').value = ""; document.getElementById('coDeadline').value = ""; document.getElementById('coNote').value = "";
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('callOffModal')).hide();
                loadContractsTab();
            }).createCallOffOrder(data);
        }
        async function sendDevAlert() {
            if (!(await showConfirm("Hệ thống sẽ quét các hợp đồng chậm tiến độ và gửi cảnh báo Telegram. Tiếp tục?"))) return;
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => { alert(res); }).checkContractDeviations();
        }

        // --- PAYMENT CALENDAR LOGIC ---
        let currentCalDate = new Date();
        let calendarData = [];

        function loadCalendar() {
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(data => {
                calendarData = data;
                renderCalendar();
            }).getCalendarData();
        }

        function renderCalendar() {
            const daysContainer = document.getElementById('calendar-days');
            if (!daysContainer) return; // [Safety Check] Exit if calendar removed

            const monthDisplay = document.getElementById('calendar-month');
            daysContainer.innerHTML = '';

            const year = currentCalDate.getFullYear();
            const month = currentCalDate.getMonth();
            monthDisplay.innerText = `Tháng ${month + 1}/${year}`;

            // Get first day of month (Adjusting for Monday start)
            let firstDay = new Date(year, month, 1).getDay();
            firstDay = (firstDay === 0) ? 6 : firstDay - 1; // 0=Sunday -> 6, 1=Monday -> 0

            const daysInMonth = new Date(year, month + 1, 0).getDate();
            const prevMonthDays = new Date(year, month, 0).getDate();

            // Previous month days
            for (let i = firstDay; i > 0; i--) {
                const dayDiv = document.createElement('div');
                dayDiv.className = 'calendar-day other-month';
                dayDiv.innerHTML = `<span class="day-number">${prevMonthDays - i + 1}</span>`;
                daysContainer.appendChild(dayDiv);
            }

            // Current month days
            for (let i = 1; i <= daysInMonth; i++) {
                const dayDiv = document.createElement('div');
                const dateStr = `${year}-${String(month + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(i).padStart(2, '0')}`;
                const isToday = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] === dateStr;

                dayDiv.className = `calendar-day ${isToday ? 'today' : ''}`;
                dayDiv.onclick = () => showCalendarDetails(dateStr);

                let dotsHtml = '<div class="dot-container">';
                const dayEvents = calendarData.filter(e => e.start === dateStr);
                dayEvents.forEach(e => {
                    dotsHtml += `<span class="dot dot-${e.type}" title="${e.title}"></span>`;
                });
                dotsHtml += '</div>';

                dayDiv.innerHTML = `<span class="day-number">${i}</span>${dotsHtml}`;
                daysContainer.appendChild(dayDiv);
            }
        }

        function changeMonth(dir) {
            currentCalDate.setMonth(currentCalDate.getMonth() + dir);
            renderCalendar();
        }

        function showCalendarDetails(dateStr) {
            const events = calendarData.filter(e => e.start === dateStr);
            const list = document.getElementById('cal-details-list');
            // Format dateStr (yyyy-mm-dd) to dd/mm/yyyy
            const parts = dateStr.split('-');
            const displayDate = parts.length === 3 ? `${parts[2]}/${parts[1]}/${parts[0]}` : dateStr;
            document.getElementById('cal-date-display').innerText = displayDate;

            if (events.length === 0) {
                list.innerHTML = '<li class="list-group-item text-center text-muted py-4">Không có khoản thu/chi nào.</li>';
            } else {
                list.innerHTML = events.map(e => {
                    let badgeClass = 'bg-secondary';
                    let label = 'SỰ KIỆN';
                    let amountDisplay = '';

                    if (e.type === 'receivable') {
                        badgeClass = 'bg-success';
                        label = 'THU';
                        amountDisplay = `<span class="fw-bold text-dark">${e.amount.toLocaleString('vi-VN')} đ</span>`;
                    } else if (e.type === 'payable') {
                        badgeClass = 'bg-danger';
                        label = 'CHI';
                        amountDisplay = `<span class="fw-bold text-dark">${e.amount.toLocaleString('vi-VN')} đ</span>`;
                    } else if (e.type === 'deadline') {
                        badgeClass = 'bg-primary';
                        label = 'HẠN GIAO';
                        amountDisplay = '<span class="badge bg-light text-primary border">Sản xuất</span>';
                    }

                    return `
                        <li class="list-group-item d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                            <div>
                                <span class="badge ${badgeClass} me-2">${label}</span>
                                <span class="fw-bold">${e.title}</span>
                            </div>
                            ${amountDisplay}
                        </li>
                    `;
                }).join('');
            }
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('calendarDetailModal')).show();
        }

        // Initialize Calendar on Dashboard load
        $('#sidebar button[data-bs-target="#dashboard"]').on('click', () => { setTimeout(loadCalendar, 300); });
        // Initial load if dashboard is default
        if (window.location.hash === '#dashboard' || !window.location.hash) { loadCalendar(); }
        // --- [NEW] ADVANCED MOBILE FEATURES ---

        // 1. Input Masking & Auto-Format
        function formatCurrency(input) {
            let val = input.value.replace(/\D/g, "");
            if (val) {
                input.value = Number(val).toLocaleString('vi-VN');
            }
        }
        function formatPhone(input) {
            let val = input.value.replace(/\D/g, "");
            let formatted = "";
            if (val.length > 0) {
                if (val.length <= 3) formatted = val;
                else if (val.length <= 6) formatted = val.substring(0, 3) + " " + val.substring(3);
                else formatted = val.substring(0, 3) + " " + val.substring(3, 6) + " " + val.substring(6, 10);
            }
            input.value = formatted;
        }

        // Apply masking to fields
        $(document).on('input', 'input[name="salesPrice"], #payPrice, #whPrice, #conPrice', function () { formatCurrency(this); });
        $(document).on('input', 'input[name="phone"], #payPhone', function () { formatPhone(this); });

        // 2. Pull-to-Refresh (PTR)
        let touchStart = 0;
        let isPTR = false;
        window.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
            if (window.scrollY === 0) touchStart = e.touches[0].pageY;
        });
        window.addEventListener('touchmove', e => {
            const touch = e.touches[0].pageY;
            const diff = touch - touchStart;
            if (window.scrollY === 0 && diff > 50) {
                isPTR = true;
                const ptr = document.getElementById('ptr-indicator');
                ptr.style.transform = `translateY(${Math.min(diff, 100)}px)`;
                ptr.querySelector('i').classList.add('bi-arrow-repeat', 'spin');
                ptr.querySelector('i').classList.remove('bi-arrow-down');
            }
        });
        window.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
            if (isPTR) {
                const ptr = document.getElementById('ptr-indicator');
                ptr.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                refreshCurrentTab();
                setTimeout(() => {
                    ptr.querySelector('i').classList.remove('bi-arrow-repeat', 'spin');
                    ptr.querySelector('i').classList.add('bi-arrow-down');
                }, 500);
            }
            isPTR = false;
        });

        // 3. Infinite Scroll / Virtual List (Simplified)
        let isLoadingMore = false;
        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
            if (window.innerHeight + window.scrollY >= document.body.offsetHeight - 200 && !isLoadingMore) {
                const activeTab = document.querySelector('.tab-pane.show.active');
                if (activeTab && (activeTab.id === 'sales' || activeTab.id === 'production')) {
                    // simulate loading more
                    console.log("Loading more entries...");
                    // In a real app, you'd fetch the next batch from the server
                }
            }
        });

        // 4. Offline Sync Engine (IndexedDB)
        const DB_NAME = "4F_ERP_OFFLINE";
        const STORE_NAME = "pending_sync";
        let db;

        const request = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, 1);
        request.onupgradeneeded = e => {
            e.target.result.createObjectStore(STORE_NAME, { keyPath: "id", autoIncrement: true });
        };
        request.onsuccess = e => { db = e.target.result; syncOfflineData(); };

        function saveOffline(action, data) {
            const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, "readwrite");
            tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).add({ action, data, timestamp: Date.now() });
            updateSyncStatus();
        }

        function updateSyncStatus() {
            const statusIndicator = document.getElementById('sync-status-indicator');
            if (navigator.onLine) {
                statusIndicator.className = "status-online";
                statusIndicator.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-cloud-check-fill"></i> Online';
            } else {
                const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, "readonly");
                const countReq = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).count();
                countReq.onsuccess = () => {
                    statusIndicator.className = "status-offline";
                    statusIndicator.innerHTML = `<i class="bi bi-cloud-slash-fill"></i> Offline (${countReq.result} chờ đồng bộ)`;
                };
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener('online', updateSyncStatus);
        window.addEventListener('offline', updateSyncStatus);

        function syncOfflineData() {
            if (!navigator.onLine || !db) return;
            const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, "readwrite");
            const store = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
            const request = store.openCursor();
            request.onsuccess = e => {
                const cursor = e.target.result;
                if (cursor) {
                    const item = cursor.value;
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(() => {
                        const deleteTx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, "readwrite");
                        deleteTx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).delete(item.id);
                        updateSyncStatus();
                    })[item.action](item.data);
                    cursor.continue();
                }
            };
        }

        // Intercept API calls to support offline
        const originalGoogleScriptRun = google.script.run;
        // This is a simplified replacement. Ideally, wrap only submission functions.
        function offlineSafeRun(action, data, successHandler) {
            if (!navigator.onLine) {
                saveOffline(action, data);
                if (successHandler) successHandler("Dữ liệu đã được lưu tạm (OFFLINE). Sẽ đồng bộ khi có mạng.");
                return;
            }
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(successHandler)[action](data);
        }

        // Add CSS for spin
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.innerHTML = `
            @keyframes spin { 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
            .spin { animation: spin 1s linear infinite; }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        updateSyncStatus();
    </script>
