    <script>
        // COSTING V21 LOGIC
        function addFabricRow(it = {}) {
            const body = document.getElementById('fabricRows');
            const row = document.createElement('tr');
            row.innerHTML = `
                <td><input type="text" class="row-input fabric-name" list="material-list" value="${it.fabric || ''}" placeholder="Tên vải..." oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="text" class="row-input fabric-color" value="${it.color || ''}" placeholder="Màu..." oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="text" class="row-input fabric-detail" value="${it.detail || ''}" placeholder="Bụng, tay..." oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="number" class="row-input fabric-qty" value="${it.qty || 1}" oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="number" class="row-input fabric-len" value="${it.len || 0}" placeholder="mm" oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="number" class="row-input fabric-wid" value="${it.wid || 0}" placeholder="mm" oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td class="text-end fw-bold fabric-row-total text-primary" style="font-size: 0.85rem;">0</td>
                <td class="text-center"><button class="remove-btn" onclick="this.closest('tr').remove(); calculateFullCosting();"><i class="bi bi-x-circle-fill"></i></button></td>
            `;
            body.appendChild(row);
        }

        function addStageRow(it = {}) {
            const body = document.getElementById('stageRows');
            const row = document.createElement('tr');
            row.innerHTML = `
                <td>
                    <select class="row-input stage-name" onchange="calculateFullCosting()">
                        <option value="Cắt Lazer" ${it.stage == 'Cắt Lazer' ? 'selected' : ''}>✂️ Cắt Lazer</option>
                        <option value="May Ráp" ${it.stage == 'May Ráp' ? 'selected' : ''}>🧵 May Ráp</option>
                        <option value="Bơm Gòn" ${it.stage == 'Bơm Gòn' ? 'selected' : ''}>☁️ Bơm Gòn</option>
                        <option value="Thêu Vi tính" ${it.stage == 'Thêu Vi tính' ? 'selected' : ''}>🪡 Thêu Vi tính</option>
                        <option value="Đóng gói" ${it.stage == 'Đóng gói' ? 'selected' : ''}>📦 Đóng gói</option>
                    </select>
                </td>
                <td><input type="number" class="row-input stage-qty" value="${it.qty || 1}" oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td><input type="number" class="row-input stage-price" value="${it.price || 5000}" oninput="calculateFullCosting()"></td>
                <td class="text-end fw-bold stage-row-total text-info" style="font-size: 0.85rem;">0</td>
                <td class="text-center"><button class="remove-btn" onclick="this.closest('tr').remove(); calculateFullCosting();"><i class="bi bi-x-circle-fill"></i></button></td>
            `;
            body.appendChild(row);
        }

        function runCostingAIScan(input) {
            if (!input.files || input.files.length === 0) return;
            const status = document.getElementById('costingAiStatus');
            status.style.display = 'block';
            status.innerText = "⏳ AI đang phân tích rập và bóc tách chi tiết...";
            
            let file = input.files[0];
            let reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = function (e) {
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        status.innerText = "✅ Đã bóc tách thành công " + res.data.length + " chi tiết!";
                        // Clear and add new rows
                        document.getElementById('fabricRows').innerHTML = "";
                        res.data.forEach(item => addFabricRow(item));
                        calculateFullCosting();
                    } else {
                        status.innerText = "❌ Lỗi: " + res.message;
                    }
                    input.value = "";
                }).analyzePdfWithGemini(e.target.result, file.type);
            };
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
        }

        function calculateFullCosting() {
            const orderQty = parseInt(document.getElementById('costOrderQty').value) || 1;
            const margin = parseFloat(document.getElementById('costMargin').value) || 30;
            const productName = $("#costProductName").data('select2') ? $("#costProductName option:selected").text().split(' (')[0] : document.getElementById('costProductName').value;
            
            let fabrics = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#fabricRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                fabrics.push({
                    fabric: tr.querySelector('.fabric-name').value,
                    color: tr.querySelector('.fabric-color').value,
                    detail: tr.querySelector('.fabric-detail').value,
                    qty: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-qty').value) || 0,
                    len: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-len').value) || 0,
                    wid: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-wid').value) || 0,
                    price: 0, // Sẽ lấy giá từ backend (Real-time)
                    fabricWidth: 1600
                });
            });

            let others = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#stageRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                const stageName = tr.querySelector('.stage-name').value;
                const qty = parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-qty').value) || 0;
                const price = parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-price').value) || 0;
                others.push({ stage: stageName, qty: qty, price: price });
            });

            const mrpLoading = document.getElementById('mrpLoading');
            if(mrpLoading) mrpLoading.style.display = 'block';

            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                if(mrpLoading) mrpLoading.style.display = 'none';
                
                document.getElementById('sumNVL').innerText = Math.round(res.totalFabricCost).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumNC').innerText = Math.round(res.totalOpCost).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumRawCost').innerText = Math.round(res.totalFabricCost + res.totalOpCost).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumMgmtFee').innerText = Math.round(res.mgmtFee).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumRiskFee').innerText = Math.round(res.riskFee).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumFinalCost').innerText = Math.round(res.finalCost).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumSellingPrice').innerText = Math.round(res.sellingPrice).toLocaleString() + " đ";
                document.getElementById('sumProfitVal').innerText = Math.round(res.sellingPrice - res.finalCost).toLocaleString();
                
                // --- Cập nhật giá trên từng dòng ---
                const fabRows = document.querySelectorAll('#fabricRows tr');
                if (res.processedFabrics) {
                    res.processedFabrics.forEach((p, idx) => {
                        if (fabRows[idx]) {
                            fabRows[idx].querySelector('.fabric-row-total').innerText = Math.round(p.totalCost).toLocaleString();
                            // Tooltip hoặc nhỏ dưới tên để biết giá gốc
                            fabRows[idx].querySelector('.fabric-name').title = "Giá gốc: " + p.unitPrice.toLocaleString() + " đ/mét";
                        }
                    });
                }

                const stageRows = document.querySelectorAll('#stageRows tr');
                if (res.processedOthers) {
                    res.processedOthers.forEach((p, idx) => {
                        if (stageRows[idx]) {
                            stageRows[idx].querySelector('.stage-row-total').innerText = Math.round(p.totalCost).toLocaleString();
                        }
                    });
                }

                // --- RENDER MRP TABLE & BUTTON ---
                let mrpHtml = ""; 
                let hasLack = false;
                res.breakdownArray.forEach(b => {
                    const statusClass = b.missing > 0 ? "text-danger fw-bold" : "text-success";
                    if (b.missing > 0) hasLack = true;
                    
                    mrpHtml += `<tr>
                        <td class="small fw-bold">${b.fullName}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">${b.demand} ${b.unit}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">${b.stock}</td>
                        <td class="text-center ${statusClass}">${b.missing > 0 ? b.missing : '-'}</td>
                    </tr>`;
                });
                
                document.getElementById('mrpTableBody').innerHTML = mrpHtml || '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center text-muted py-3">Chưa có dữ liệu...</td></tr>';
                
                const btnPur = document.getElementById('btnCreateRequest');
                if (btnPur) btnPur.style.display = hasLack ? 'block' : 'none';
                
                // Thu thập Order ID từ dropdown
                const $sel = $("#costProductName");
                const currentOrderId = $sel.val();
                
                window.currentBreakdownData = { 
                    items: res.breakdownArray, 
                    productName: productName, 
                    orderId: currentOrderId 
                };

            }).runCalculations({ orderQty, margin, fabrics, others });
        }

        async function submitQuickPurchase() {
            if (!window.currentBreakdownData) return;
            const lackCount = window.currentBreakdownData.items.filter(i => i.missing > 0).length;
            if (lackCount === 0) return Swal.fire({icon:'success', title:'Kho đủ hàng!', text:'Tồn kho hiện tại đã đủ vải cho đơn này, không cần mua thêm!', timer:2500});
            
            if (!(await showConfirm("Hệ thống sẽ tạo " + lackCount + " yêu cầu mua hàng cho dự án này. Tiếp tục?"))) return;
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('btnCreateRequest');
            const oldText = btn.innerHTML;
            btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Đang gửi...';
            btn.disabled = true;
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                alert(res);
                btn.innerHTML = oldText;
                btn.disabled = false;
            }).submitMaterialRequestFromCosting(window.currentBreakdownData);
        }

        function resetCostingForm(force = false) {
            const clear = () => {
                $('#costProductName').val(null).trigger('change');
                document.getElementById('costOrderQty').value = 1;
                document.getElementById('costMargin').value = 30;
                document.getElementById('fabricRows').innerHTML = "";
                document.getElementById('stageRows').innerHTML = "";
                document.getElementById('imgPreviewBox').style.backgroundImage = "none";
                document.getElementById('imgPreviewBox').innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-image fs-2"></i><span class="small fw-bold">Ảnh SP</span><input type="file" id="costProductImg" class="d-none" onchange="previewCostingImg(this)">';
                addFabricRow();
                addStageRow();
                // Reset summary display via calculation
                setTimeout(calculateFullCosting, 100);
            };

            if (force) {
                clear();
            } else {
                showAsk("Xóa trắng toàn bộ dữ liệu đang nhập?", clear);
            }
        }

        function previewCostingImg(input) {
            if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
                let reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function (e) {
                    const box = document.getElementById('imgPreviewBox');
                    box.style.backgroundImage = `url(${e.target.result})`;
                    box.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
                    box.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
                    box.innerHTML = '<input type="file" id="costProductImg" class="d-none" onchange="previewCostingImg(this)">';
                }
                reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
            }
        }

        function saveFullCostingToDatabase() {
            const $select = $('#costProductName');
            const orderId = $select.val();
            let productName = "";
            
            if (orderId && window.activeOrdersForCosting) {
                const order = window.activeOrdersForCosting.find(o => o.id == orderId);
                if (order) productName = order.product;
            } else {
                productName = $select.val(); // Nếu thợ tự nhập tay vào select2tags
            }
            
            if (!productName || productName.includes("-- Chọn")) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Chưa chọn sản phẩm', text:'Vui lòng chọn hoặc nhập tên sản phẩm trước khi lưu định mức!', timer:2500});
            
            const btn = event.target;
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.innerText = "⏳ ĐANG LƯU...";

            // Thu thập dữ liệu để lưu (Logic tương tự như calculateFullCosting nhưng gửi đi để lưu)
            const orderQty = parseInt(document.getElementById('costOrderQty').value) || 1;
            const margin = parseFloat(document.getElementById('costMargin').value) || 30;
            
            let fabrics = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#fabricRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                const fabric = tr.querySelector('.fabric-name').value;
                if(fabric) {
                    fabrics.push({
                        fabric: fabric,
                        color: tr.querySelector('.fabric-color').value,
                        detail: tr.querySelector('.fabric-detail').value,
                        qty: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-qty').value) || 0,
                        len: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-len').value) || 0,
                        wid: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-wid').value) || 0,
                        price: 80000,
                        fabricWidth: 1600
                    });
                }
            });

            let stages = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#stageRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                stages.push({
                    stage: tr.querySelector('.stage-name').value,
                    qty: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-qty').value) || 0,
                    price: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-price').value) || 0
                });
            });

            const costingData = {
                productName,
                orderQty,
                margin,
                fabrics,
                stages,
                totalCost: document.getElementById('sumFinalCost').innerText,
                sellingPrice: document.getElementById('sumSellingPrice').innerText
            };

            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                showMsg("✅ " + res);
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.innerText = "LƯU ĐỊNH MỨC";
            }).saveFullCostingData(costingData);
        }

        // --- QUOTATION CONVERSION LOGIC ---
        function convertCostingToOrder() {
            const $select = $('#costProductName');
            let productName = "";
            const selectVal = $select.val();
            
            // 1. Resolve Product Name
            if (selectVal && window.activeOrdersForCosting) {
                const order = window.activeOrdersForCosting.find(o => o.id == selectVal);
                if (order) productName = order.product;
                else productName = selectVal; // New tag
            } else {
                productName = selectVal;
            }
            
            // Fallback: Check Select2 displayed text
            if (!productName || productName.includes("-- Chọn")) {
                try {
                    const selData = $select.select2('data');
                    if (selData && selData.length > 0) {
                        let fullText = selData[0].text;
                        if (fullText.includes(" - ")) {
                            productName = fullText.split(" - ")[1].split(" (")[0];
                        } else {
                            productName = fullText;
                        }
                    }
                } catch(e) { console.error("Select2 Error:", e); }
            }
            
            if (!productName || productName.includes("-- Chọn") || productName.trim() === "") {
                return showMsg("Vui lòng nhập tên sản phẩm trước khi chốt đơn!", 'warning');
            }
            
            const qty = document.getElementById('costOrderQty').value;
            const priceStr = document.getElementById('sumSellingPrice').innerText.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
            const price = parseInt(priceStr) || 0;
            
            document.getElementById('ctoProduct').value = productName;
            document.getElementById('ctoQty').value = qty;
            document.getElementById('ctoPrice').value = price;
            setFlatpickrDate('ctoDate', new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]);
            
            // Populate Dropdowns
            const custSelect = document.getElementById('ctoCustomer');
            const saleSelect = document.getElementById('ctoSalesRep');
            
            custSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Chọn Khách --</option>';
            if (window.customerMap) {
                for (let n in window.customerMap) {
                    custSelect.add(new Option(n, n));
                }
            }
            
            const salesList = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#salesSelect option').forEach(opt => {
                if (opt.value) salesList.push(opt.value);
            });
            saleSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Chọn Sale --</option>';
            salesList.forEach(s => saleSelect.add(new Option(s, s)));
            
            const modal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('costToOrderModal'));
            modal.show();
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                $('.select2-cto').select2({ theme: 'bootstrap-5', width: '100%', dropdownParent: $('#costToOrderModal') });
            }, 300);
        }

        function updateAddressCTO() {
            const customer = document.getElementById('ctoCustomer').value;
            if (window.customerMap && window.customerMap[customer]) {
                const data = window.customerMap[customer];
                document.getElementById('ctoAddress').value = data[0] || "";
                document.getElementById('ctoPhone').value = data[1] || "";
            }
        }

        async function submitOrderFromCosting(btn) {
            const productName = document.getElementById('ctoProduct').value;
            const customer = document.getElementById('ctoCustomer').value;
            const salesRep = document.getElementById('ctoSalesRep').value;
            const qty = document.getElementById('ctoQty').value;
            const price = document.getElementById('ctoPrice').value;
            const deadline = document.getElementById('ctoDeadline').value;
            
            if (!customer || !qty || !price || !deadline) return showMsg("Vui lòng điền đầy đủ các thông tin (*)", 'warning');
            
            if (!(await showConfirm("Hệ thống sẽ tạo đơn hàng mới và lưu định mức này cho sản phẩm. Tiếp tục?"))) return;
            
            if (btn) {
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> ĐANG XỬ LÝ...';
            }
            
            const orderData = {
                orderDate: document.getElementById('ctoDate').value,
                deadline: deadline,
                customer: customer,
                salesRep: salesRep,
                productName: productName,
                quantity: qty,
                salesPrice: price,
                address: document.getElementById('ctoAddress').value,
                phone: document.getElementById('ctoPhone').value,
                notes: document.getElementById('ctoNote').value,
                imageUrl: "" 
            };
            
            let fabrics = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#fabricRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                const fbName = tr.querySelector('.fabric-name').value;
                if(fbName) {
                    fabrics.push({
                        fabric: fbName,
                        color: tr.querySelector('.fabric-color').value,
                        detail: tr.querySelector('.fabric-detail').value,
                        qty: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-qty').value) || 0,
                        len: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-len').value) || 0,
                        wid: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.fabric-wid').value) || 0,
                        price: 0,
                        fabricWidth: 1600
                    });
                }
            });

            let stages = [];
            document.querySelectorAll('#stageRows tr').forEach(tr => {
                stages.push({
                    stage: tr.querySelector('.stage-name').value,
                    qty: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-qty').value) || 0,
                    price: parseFloat(tr.querySelector('.stage-price').value) || 0
                });
            });

            const costingData = {
                productName,
                orderQty: qty,
                margin: document.getElementById('costMargin').value,
                fabrics,
                stages,
                totalCost: document.getElementById('sumFinalCost').innerText,
                sellingPrice: document.getElementById('sumSellingPrice').innerText
            };

            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(resCost => {
                    google.script.run
                        .withSuccessHandler(resOrder => {
                            showMsg("✅ " + resOrder + "\n" + resCost);
                            bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('costToOrderModal')).hide();
                            
                            // Reset form định mức để nhập tiếp
                            resetCostingForm(true);

                            const salesBtn = document.querySelector('#sidebar button[data-bs-target="#sales"]');
                            if (salesBtn) salesBtn.click();
                            setTimeout(loadSalesHistory, 1000);
                        })
                        .withFailureHandler(err => {
                            showMsg("Lỗi tạo đơn hàng: " + err, 'error');
                            if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = 'XÁC NHẬN LÊN ĐƠN'; }
                        })
                        .submitOrder(orderData);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(err => {
                    showMsg("Lỗi lưu định mức: " + err, 'error');
                    if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = 'XÁC NHẬN LÊN ĐƠN'; }
                })
                .saveFullCostingData(costingData);
        }

        // Khởi tạo dòng mặc định
        window.addEventListener('load', () => { setTimeout(() => { addFabricRow(); addStageRow(); }, 2000); });
        // --- MISA IMPORT SCRIPT ---
        let currentInvoiceData = [];

        function previewMisaFile() {
            const file = document.getElementById('misaFile').files[0];
            if(!file) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Chưa chọn file', text:'Vui lòng chọn file Excel xuất từ phần mềm MISA!', timer:2500});
            
            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = function(e) {
                const data = new Uint8Array(e.target.result);
                const workbook = XLSX.read(data, {type: 'array'});
                const firstSheetName = workbook.SheetNames[0];
                const worksheet = workbook.Sheets[firstSheetName];
                
                let rows = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(worksheet, { header: 1 });
                let headerRowIndex = -1;
                
                for(let i = 0; i < Math.min(rows.length, 20); i++){
                    if(rows[i] && rows[i].join('').toLowerCase().includes('số hóa đơn')){
                        headerRowIndex = i; break;
                    }
                }
                
                if (headerRowIndex === -1) {
                    return Swal.fire({icon:'error', title:'File không hợp lệ', text:"File không phải định dạng MISA hoặc thiếu cột 'Số hóa đơn'. Vui lòng kiểm tra lại!"});
                }

                const headers = rows[headerRowIndex].map(h => (h || '').toString().toLowerCase().trim());

                const colTen = headers.findIndex(h => h === 'tên đơn vị' || h === 'tên người bán' || h === 'tên khách hàng' || h === 'nhà cung cấp' || (h.includes('tên') && !h.includes('mã số thuế')));
                const colMST = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('mã số thuế') || h.includes('mst'));
                const colSoHD = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('số hóa đơn') || h.includes('số hd'));
                const colNgay = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('ngày'));
                const colTienTruocThue = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('chưa có thuế') || h.includes('chưa thuế') || h.includes('doanh số'));
                const colVATRate = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('thuế suất') || h.includes('%'));
                const colTienThue = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('tiền thuế'));
                const colTongTien = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('tổng cộng') || h.includes('đã có thuế') || h.includes('tổng tiền'));

                if (colSoHD === -1 || colNgay === -1) {
                    return Swal.fire({icon:'error', title:'File thiếu cột bắt buộc', text:'Không tìm thấy cột Số HĐ hoặc Ngày trong file. Vui lòng kiểm tra lại file MISA!'});
                }

                currentInvoiceData = [];
                for(let i = headerRowIndex + 1; i < rows.length; i++){
                    let r = rows[i];
                    if (!r || r.length === 0) continue;
                    let soHD = r[colSoHD];
                    if (!soHD) continue; 

                    let ngayText = r[colNgay]; 
                    if (typeof ngayText === 'number' && ngayText > 40000) { 
                        let d = new Date((ngayText - (25567 + 1)) * 86400 * 1000); 
                        ngayText = d.toISOString().split('T')[0];
                    } else if (ngayText instanceof Date) {
                        ngayText = ngayText.toISOString().split('T')[0];
                    }

                    const safeMoney = (v) => {
                        if (!v) return 0;
                        if (typeof v === 'number') return v;
                        return parseFloat(v.toString().replace(/,/g, '').replace(/\./g, '')) || 0;
                    };
                    const safeStr = (v) => v ? v.toString().trim() : '';

                    currentInvoiceData.push({
                        invoiceNumber: safeStr(soHD),
                        invoiceDate: safeStr(ngayText),
                        taxCode: colMST !== -1 ? safeStr(r[colMST]) : '',
                        companyName: colTen !== -1 ? safeStr(r[colTen]) : '',
                        netAmount: colTienTruocThue !== -1 ? safeMoney(r[colTienTruocThue]) : 0,
                        vatPercentage: colVATRate !== -1 ? safeStr(r[colVATRate]) : '',
                        taxAmount: colTienThue !== -1 ? safeMoney(r[colTienThue]) : 0,
                        totalAmount: colTongTien !== -1 ? safeMoney(r[colTongTien]) : 0
                    });
                }
                
                let html = '';
                let totalNet = 0, totalTax = 0, totalAll = 0;

                currentInvoiceData.forEach(inv => {
                    totalNet += inv.netAmount;
                    totalTax += inv.taxAmount;
                    totalAll += inv.totalAmount;

                    html += `<tr>
                        <td class="fw-bold">${inv.invoiceNumber}</td>
                        <td>${inv.invoiceDate}</td>
                        <td>${inv.taxCode}</td>
                        <td class="small fw-bold" style="min-width:200px">${inv.companyName}</td>
                        <td class="text-end text-success">${inv.netAmount.toLocaleString()}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">${inv.vatPercentage}</td>
                        <td class="text-end text-warning">${inv.taxAmount.toLocaleString()}</td>
                        <td class="text-end fw-bold text-primary">${inv.totalAmount.toLocaleString()}</td>
                    </tr>`;
                });
                
                // Thêm dòng tổng cộng
                html += `<tr class="table-info fw-bold">
                    <td colspan="4" class="text-center text-uppercase">Tổng cộng (${currentInvoiceData.length} hóa đơn)</td>
                    <td class="text-end text-success">${totalNet.toLocaleString()}</td>
                    <td></td>
                    <td class="text-end text-warning">${totalTax.toLocaleString()}</td>
                    <td class="text-end text-primary" style="font-size: 1.1rem">${totalAll.toLocaleString()}</td>
                </tr>`;
                

                
                document.getElementById('previewTableMisaBody').innerHTML = html;
                document.getElementById('misaPreviewZone').style.display = 'block';
                Swal.fire({ icon: 'success', title: 'Đọc file thành công', text: `Tìm thấy ${currentInvoiceData.length} hóa đơn hợp lệ.`, timer: 2000, showConfirmButton: false });
            };
            reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);
        }

        function confirmImportMisa() {
            if (!currentInvoiceData || currentInvoiceData.length === 0) return Swal.fire({icon:'warning', title:'Chưa có dữ liệu', text:'Vui lòng chọn và xem trước file trước khi import!', timer:2500});
            const type = document.getElementById('invoiceType').value;
            const btn = document.getElementById('btnConfirmMisaImport');
            
            Swal.fire({
                title: 'Xác nhận tích hợp?',
                text: `Sẽ import ${currentInvoiceData.length} hóa đơn vào hệ thống!`,
                icon: 'warning',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonColor: '#3085d6',
                cancelButtonColor: '#d33',
                confirmButtonText: 'Đồng ý'
            }).then((result) => {
                if (result.isConfirmed) {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.innerHTML = `<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> ĐANG XỬ LÝ...`;
                    
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                        btn.disabled = false;
                        btn.innerHTML = `<i class="bi bi-cloud-arrow-up"></i> TÍCH HỢP VÀO HỆ THỐNG`;
                        document.getElementById('misaPreviewZone').style.display = 'none';
                        document.getElementById('misaFile').value = '';
                        currentInvoiceData = [];
                        
                        Swal.fire('Hoàn tất!', res.message, res.status);
                        
                        // Cập nhật lại biểu đồ nếu đang mở
                        loadVatDashboard();
                    }).withFailureHandler(err => {
                        window.alert("Lỗi máy chủ: " + err.message);
                        btn.disabled = false;
                        btn.innerHTML = `<i class="bi bi-cloud-arrow-up"></i> TÍCH HỢP VÀO HỆ THỐNG`;
                    }).importMisaInvoicesBackend(currentInvoiceData, type);
                }
            });
        }

        function openInvoiceManager() {
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('invoiceManagerModal')).show();
            fetchInvoicesForManager();
        }

        function fetchInvoicesForManager() {
            const type = document.querySelector('input[name="mgrInvType"]:checked').value;
            const body = document.getElementById('invoiceManagerTableBody');
            body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-4"><div class="spinner-border text-info"></div><br>Đang tải dữ liệu...</td></tr>';
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                if (!list || list.length === 0) {
                    body.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-4 text-muted">Chưa có dữ liệu hóa đơn nào được import.</td></tr>';
                    return;
                }
                
                let html = '';
                list.forEach(inv => {
                    html += `<tr>
                        <td class="text-center fw-bold text-secondary">${inv.importDate}</td>
                        <td class="text-center fw-bold">${inv.invoiceNumber}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">${inv.invoiceDate}</td>
                        <td class="fw-bold">${inv.companyName}</td>
                        <td class="text-end fw-bold text-primary">${inv.totalAmount.toLocaleString()}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">
                            <button class="btn btn-link text-danger p-0" onclick="deleteInvoiceFromManager('${inv.invoiceNumber}', '${inv.companyName}', '${inv.invoiceDate}')">
                                <i class="bi bi-trash-fill"></i> Xóa
                            </button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`;
                });
                body.innerHTML = html;
            }).getImportedInvoicesBackend(type);
        }

        function deleteInvoiceFromManager(num, company, date) {
            const type = document.querySelector('input[name="mgrInvType"]:checked').value;
            
            Swal.fire({
                title: 'Xác nhận xóa?',
                text: `Hóa đơn ${num} của ${company} sẽ bị gỡ bỏ khỏi hệ thống.`,
                icon: 'warning',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonText: 'Đồng ý xóa'
            }).then(result => {
                if (result.isConfirmed) {
                    Swal.showLoading();
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                        Swal.fire('Thành công', res.message, 'success');
                        fetchInvoicesForManager();
                        loadVatDashboard(); // Cập nhật biểu đồ
                    }).deleteMisaInvoice(num, company, date, type);
                }
            });
        }

        // --- DASHBOARD VAT & PNL MISA ---
        let vatChartInstance = null;
        let pnlChartInstance = null;

        function loadVatDashboard() {
            const btn = (event && event.target) ? event.target.closest('.btn') : null;
            if(btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm"></span> Tải...'; }
            
            const startDate = document.getElementById('acc-start-date').value;
            const endDate = document.getElementById('acc-end-date').value;
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                if(btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-arrow-clockwise"></i> Load Dữ Liệu'; }
                
                if (!res || !res.monthly) return;
                
                const formatMoney = v => new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN').format(v) + " ₫";
                document.getElementById('v-rev').innerText = formatMoney(res.summary.revenue);
                document.getElementById('v-exp').innerText = formatMoney(res.summary.expense);
                document.getElementById('v-profit').innerText = formatMoney(res.summary.profit);
                
                const vatEl = document.getElementById('v-vatDiff');
                const vatDesc = document.getElementById('v-vatDesc');
                vatEl.innerText = formatMoney(Math.abs(res.summary.vatDiff));
                if (res.summary.vatDiff > 0) {
                    vatEl.className = "fs-4 fw-bold text-danger mt-2";
                    vatDesc.innerHTML = "VAT PHẢI NỘP NĂM NAY <i class='bi bi-arrow-down-right-circle text-danger'></i>";
                } else {
                    vatEl.className = "fs-4 fw-bold text-success mt-2";
                    vatDesc.innerHTML = "VAT ĐANG KHẤU TRỪ <i class='bi bi-arrow-up-right-circle text-success'></i>";
                }

                renderVatChart(res.monthly);
                renderPnlChart(res.monthly);
                
            }).withFailureHandler(err => {
                if(btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-arrow-clockwise"></i> Load Dữ Liệu'; }
                console.error(err);
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Không thể tải dữ liệu Dashboard VAT', 'error');
            }).getVatAndPnlData(startDate, endDate);
        }

        function renderVatChart(data) {
            const options = {
                series: [{ name: 'VAT Đầu Ra (Phải nộp)', data: data.vatOut }, { name: 'VAT Đầu Vào (Được khấu trừ)', data: data.vatIn }],
                chart: { type: 'bar', height: 300, toolbar: { show: false } },
                plotOptions: { bar: { horizontal: false, columnWidth: '55%', endingShape: 'rounded' } },
                dataLabels: { enabled: false },
                stroke: { show: true, width: 2, colors: ['transparent'] },
                xaxis: { categories: data.labels },
                yaxis: { title: { text: 'Triệu VNĐ' }, labels: { formatter: (value) => { return (value/1000000).toFixed(0) + "M"; } } },
                fill: { opacity: 1 },
                colors: ['#dc3545', '#198754'],
                title: { text: 'Cân Đối Thuế GTGT (VAT) Hàng Tháng', align: 'left', style: { fontSize: '14px', fontWeight: 'bold' } },
                tooltip: { y: { formatter: function (val) { return new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN').format(val) + " đ" } } }
            };

            if (vatChartInstance) vatChartInstance.destroy();
            vatChartInstance = new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chartVatBalance"), options);
            vatChartInstance.render();
        }

        function renderPnlChart(data) {
            const options = {
                series: [{ name: 'Tổng Doanh Thu', data: data.rev }, { name: 'Tổng Chi Tiền Hàng', data: data.exp }],
                chart: { type: 'line', height: 300, toolbar: { show: false } },
                stroke: { width: 3, curve: 'smooth' },
                xaxis: { categories: data.labels },
                yaxis: { title: { text: 'Triệu VNĐ' }, labels: { formatter: (value) => { return (value/1000000).toFixed(0) + "M"; } } },
                colors: ['#0d6efd', '#ffc107'],
                title: { text: 'Doanh Thu Quá Khứ vs Chi Phí Nhập Hàng', align: 'left', style: { fontSize: '14px', fontWeight: 'bold' } },
                markers: { size: 4 },
                tooltip: { y: { formatter: function (val) { return new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN').format(val) + " đ" } } }
            };

            if (pnlChartInstance) pnlChartInstance.destroy();
            pnlChartInstance = new ApexCharts(document.querySelector("#chartPnlMisa"), options);
            pnlChartInstance.render();
        }

        // --- ORDER COST REPORT LOGIC ---
        function loadOrderCostReportTab() {
            const select = document.getElementById('cost-order-select');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">--- Đang tải danh sách... ---</option>';
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(list => {
                let html = '<option value="">--- Chọn Đơn Hàng ---</option>';
                list.forEach(o => {
                    html += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.id} - ${o.customer} (${o.product})</option>`;
                });
                select.innerHTML = html;
            }).getAllOrderList();
        }

        function fetchOrderCostReport() {
            const id = document.getElementById('cost-order-select').value;
            if (!id) return;
            
            Swal.fire({ 
                title: 'Đang trích xuất dữ liệu...', 
                allowOutsideClick: false, 
                didOpen: () => { Swal.showLoading(); } 
            });
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.close();
                if (res.error) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', res.error, 'error');
                
                document.getElementById('cost-report-content').style.display = 'block';
                
                // Summary
                const formatVnd = (v) => v.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " đ";
                document.getElementById('cost-revenue').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.revenue);
                document.getElementById('cost-total-expense').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.totalCost);
                document.getElementById('cost-profit').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.profit);
                document.getElementById('cost-margin').innerText = res.summary.profitMargin + '%';
                document.getElementById('cost-oh-allocation').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.ohCost || 0);

                // Advanced Costing Fields
                document.getElementById('cost-produced-qty').innerText = res.summary.totalProducedQty || 0;
                document.getElementById('cost-actual-unit').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.actualUnitCost || 0);
                document.getElementById('cost-standard-unit').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.standardUnitCost || 0);
                
                const variance = res.summary.variance || 0;
                const varElem = document.getElementById('cost-variance');
                const varCard = document.getElementById('cost-variance-card');
                
                varElem.innerText = (variance > 0 ? "+" : "") + formatVnd(variance);
                if (variance > 0) {
                    varCard.style.background = '#fef2f2'; // Đỏ nhạt (Over budget)
                    varElem.style.color = '#dc2626';
                } else if (variance < 0) {
                    varCard.style.background = '#f0fdf4'; // Xanh nhạt (Under budget)
                    varElem.style.color = '#16a34a';
                } else {
                    varCard.style.background = '#f8fafc';
                    varElem.style.color = '#334155';
                }
                
                // Profit card color change
                const profitCard = document.getElementById('cost-profit').parentElement;
                if (res.summary.profit < 0) {
                    profitCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#b91c1c)';
                } else {
                    profitCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#10b981,#059669)';
                }
                
                // Header info
                document.getElementById('cost-cust').innerText = res.order.customer;
                document.getElementById('cost-prod').innerText = res.order.product;
                document.getElementById('cost-qty').innerText = res.order.qty;
                document.getElementById('cost-status').innerText = res.order.status;
                document.getElementById('cost-paid').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.realizedRevenue);
                
                // Cost Breakdown Visual Bars
                renderCostBreakdownBars(res.summary);
                
                // Material Table
                let matHtml = '';
                res.matCosts.forEach(m => {
                    let typeBadge = '';
                    let rowStyle = '';
                    if (m.type === 'Nhập kho') {
                        typeBadge = '<span class="badge bg-secondary">Nhập kho</span>';
                        rowStyle = 'style="opacity: 0.6; background: #f9f9f9;"';
                    } else if (m.type === 'Xuất kho') {
                        typeBadge = '<span class="badge bg-danger">Xuất kho</span>';
                    } else {
                        typeBadge = '<span class="badge bg-info">Sản xuất</span>';
                    }
                    matHtml += `<tr ${rowStyle}><td>${m.date}</td><td>${typeBadge} ${m.name}</td><td>${m.qty} ${m.unit}</td><td class="text-end">${m.price.toLocaleString()}</td><td class="text-end fw-bold">${m.total.toLocaleString()}</td></tr>`;
                });
                document.getElementById('cost-mat-body').innerHTML = matHtml || '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center">Không có log vật tư</td></tr>';
                document.getElementById('cost-total-mat').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.matCost);
                
                // Labor Table
                let laborHtml = '';
                res.laborCosts.forEach(l => {
                    laborHtml += `<tr><td>${l.date}</td><td>${l.worker}</td><td>${l.stage}</td><td>${l.qty}</td><td class="text-end fw-bold">${l.total.toLocaleString()}</td></tr>`;
                });
                document.getElementById('cost-labor-body').innerHTML = laborHtml || '<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center">Không có log nhân công</td></tr>';
                document.getElementById('cost-total-labor').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.laborCost);
                
                // Other Table (Finance)
                let otherHtml = '';
                res.otherCosts.forEach(o => {
                    otherHtml += `<tr><td>${o.date}</td><td>${o.category}</td><td class="text-end fw-bold">${o.amount.toLocaleString()}</td><td>${o.note}</td></tr>`;
                });
                document.getElementById('cost-other-body').innerHTML = otherHtml || '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center">Không có chi phí khác</td></tr>';
                document.getElementById('cost-total-other').innerText = formatVnd(res.summary.otherCost);
                

                renderManualCostsTable(res.manualCosts || [], res.summary.manualCost || 0);
                
            }).getOrderCostReport(id);
        }


        function renderManualCostsTable(manualCosts, totalManualCost) {
            const formatVnd = (v) => v.toLocaleString('vi-VN') + " đ";
            const typeIcons = {
                'Vận chuyển':'🚛', 'Đóng gói / Bao bì':'📦', 'Gia công ngoài':'🏭',
                'Vật tư bổ sung':'🧶', 'Chi phí chung (OH)':'⚙️', 'Khác':'📝'
            };
            
            let manualHtml = '';
            if (manualCosts.length > 0) {
                manualCosts.forEach(mc => {
                    const icon = typeIcons[mc.type] || '💰';
                    manualHtml += `<tr>
                        <td>${mc.date}</td>
                        <td><span class="badge" style="background:#8b5cf6">${icon} ${mc.type}</span></td>
                        <td>${mc.category}</td>
                        <td class="text-end fw-bold" style="color:#6d28d9">${mc.amount.toLocaleString()}</td>
                        <td class="small text-muted">${mc.note}</td>
                        <td class="text-center">
                            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" onclick="deleteManualCost('${mc.id}')" title="Xóa">
                                <i class="bi bi-trash"></i>
                            </button>
                        </td>
                    </tr>`;
                });
                document.getElementById('cost-manual-empty').style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                document.getElementById('cost-manual-empty').style.display = 'block';
            }
            document.getElementById('cost-manual-body').innerHTML = manualHtml;
            document.getElementById('cost-total-manual-badge').innerText = formatVnd(totalManualCost);
        }


        function renderCostBreakdownBars(summary) {
            const total = summary.totalCost || 1;
            const items = [
                { label: 'Vật tư', value: summary.matCost, color: '#ef4444' },
                { label: 'Nhân công', value: summary.laborCost, color: '#f59e0b' },
                { label: 'Finance', value: summary.otherCost, color: '#6b7280' },
                { label: 'Thủ công', value: summary.manualCost || 0, color: '#8b5cf6' }
            ];
            
            let html = '';
            items.forEach(item => {
                const pct = total > 0 ? ((item.value / total) * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;
                html += `<div class="mb-2">
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between small fw-bold mb-1">
                        <span>${item.label}</span>
                        <span>${item.value.toLocaleString('vi-VN')} đ (${pct}%)</span>
                    </div>
                    <div style="background:#e2e8f0; border-radius:4px; height:8px; overflow:hidden;">
                        <div style="width:${pct}%; background:${item.color}; height:100%; border-radius:4px; transition:width 0.5s ease;"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            document.getElementById('cost-breakdown-bars').innerHTML = html;
        }


        function openAddCostModal() {
            const orderId = document.getElementById('cost-order-select').value;
            if (!orderId) {
                Swal.fire('Chưa chọn đơn', 'Vui lòng chọn đơn hàng trước khi thêm chi phí.', 'warning');
                return;
            }
            const selectedText = document.getElementById('cost-order-select').selectedOptions[0].text;
            document.getElementById('cost-modal-order-info').innerHTML = 
                `<i class="bi bi-box-seam"></i> Đang thêm chi phí cho: <b>${selectedText}</b>`;
            
            // Reset form
            document.getElementById('mc-type').value = 'VAN_CHUYEN';
            document.getElementById('mc-category').value = '';
            document.getElementById('mc-amount').value = '';
            document.getElementById('mc-note').value = '';
            
            new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('addCostModal')).show();
        }


        function submitManualCost() {
            const orderId = document.getElementById('cost-order-select').value;
            const type = document.getElementById('mc-type').value;
            const category = document.getElementById('mc-category').value;
            const amount = document.getElementById('mc-amount').value;
            const note = document.getElementById('mc-note').value;
            
            if (!orderId) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Chưa chọn đơn hàng!', 'error');
            if (!amount || Number(amount) <= 0) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Số tiền phải lớn hơn 0!', 'error');
            
            Swal.fire({ title: 'Đang lưu...', allowOutsideClick: false, didOpen: () => Swal.showLoading() });
            
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                Swal.close();
                bootstrap.Modal.getInstance(document.getElementById('addCostModal'))?.hide();
                Swal.fire({ icon: 'success', title: 'Thành công', text: res, timer: 2000, showConfirmButton: false });
                // Reload report
                setTimeout(() => fetchOrderCostReport(), 500);
            }).withFailureHandler(err => {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi hệ thống', err.message, 'error');
            }).submitOrderCost({
                orderId: orderId,
                type: type,
                category: category || undefined,
                amount: Number(amount),
                note: note,
                createdBy: (window.currentRole || 'User')
            });
        }


        function deleteManualCost(costId) {
            Swal.fire({
                title: 'Xóa chi phí?',
                text: 'Mã: ' + costId + ' - Hành động này không thể hoàn tác!',
                icon: 'warning',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonColor: '#dc3545',
                confirmButtonText: 'Xóa',
                cancelButtonText: 'Hủy'
            }).then(result => {
                if (result.isConfirmed) {
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'Đang xóa...', allowOutsideClick: false, didOpen: () => Swal.showLoading() });
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(res => {
                        Swal.fire({ icon: 'success', title: 'Đã xóa', text: res, timer: 1500, showConfirmButton: false });
                        setTimeout(() => fetchOrderCostReport(), 500);
                    }).withFailureHandler(err => {
                        Swal.fire('Lỗi', err.message, 'error');
                    }).deleteOrderCost(costId);
                }
            });
        }

        // Tự động tải Dashboard khi vào Tab Kế Toán
        document.querySelector('button[onclick="switchTab(\'acc\')"]')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            setTimeout(() => { if (!vatChartInstance) loadVatDashboard(); }, 500);
        });

        // -- BỔ SUNG UI INTERACTIONS -- //
        function triggerToast(title, message, type = 'success') {
            const container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
            if(!container) return;
            const elm = document.createElement('div');
            const bgClass = (type === 'error') ? 'toast-error' : 'toast-success';
            const iconClass = (type === 'error') ? 'bi-exclamation-triangle-fill text-danger' : 'bi-check-circle-fill text-success';
            
            elm.className = `toast-msg ${bgClass}`;
            elm.innerHTML = `
                <div class="toast-icon"><i class="bi ${iconClass} fs-5"></i></div>
                <div class="toast-content">
                    <div class="toast-title">${title}</div>
                    <div class="toast-desc">${message}</div>
                </div>
            `;
            container.appendChild(elm);
            setTimeout(() => elm.classList.add('show'), 10);
            setTimeout(() => {
                elm.classList.remove('show');
                setTimeout(() => elm.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        function toggleExpandRow(element) {
            const tr = element.closest('tr');
            const nextTr = tr.nextElementSibling;
            if (nextTr && nextTr.classList.contains('expand-row')) {
                if (nextTr.classList.contains('open')) {
                    nextTr.classList.remove('open');
                    tr.classList.remove('row-open');
                } else {
                    nextTr.classList.add('open');
                    tr.classList.add('row-open');
                }
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>
